---
title: "Tool Library"
icon: "books"
description: "Explore plug-and-play tools for your AI agents"
---

## Overview

The Tool Library provides ready-made integrations that your AI agents can use during conversations. No coding required—just add the tool, configure the settings, and your agent can book appointments, send messages, fetch data, and more.

<Tip>
  **How it works:** When you add a tool to your agent, it becomes available for
  the agent to call during conversations. The agent decides when to use each
  tool based on your prompt instructions.
</Tip>

---

## Variables vs Configurations

Understanding the difference between variables and configurations is key to using tools effectively.

<CardGroup cols={2}>
  <Card title="Variables" icon="wand-sparkles">
    **Filled by the agent during the conversation** The agent gathers this
    information from the customer and passes it to the tool. **Examples:** -
    Customer's name - Preferred appointment time - Email address - Phone number
  </Card>

  <Card title="Configurations" icon="gear">
    **Preset when you add the tool** You configure these once, and they stay the
    same for every call/chat. **Examples:** - API keys - Calendar IDs - Default
    timezone - Integration credentials
  </Card>
</CardGroup>

**Example:**

When using the "Fetch Free Slots" tool:

- **Configuration:** You set the Calendar ID once (which calendar to check)
- **Variables:** The agent fills in the start_date and timezone during each conversation

---

## Popular Tools

Commonly used tools that work across all industries.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Book AI Callback" icon="phone-arrow-up-right">
    Allow your agents to schedule callbacks—the agent will automatically call the user back at the specified time.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `call_time` – Local time to call back in ISO 8601 format *(required)*
    - `timezone` – Timezone in IANA format *(required)*
    - `first_message` – Opening line when callback connects *(optional)*

    <Tip>
      Example first message: "Hi again! This is Sarah from Elite Fitness calling back as promised. Do you have a minute now?"
    </Tip>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Current Time" icon="clock">
    Get the current time for any timezone in ISO 8601 format.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `timezone` – Timezone in IANA format *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Send Twilio SMS" icon="message">
    Send text messages directly from your agent using your Twilio account.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `to_number` – Phone number in international format *(required)*
    - `message` – The SMS message content *(required)*

    <Note>
      Remember: US SMS requires A2P registration. See the [Telephony guide](/telephony) for details.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Send SendGrid Email" icon="envelope">
    Send emails directly from your agent using SendGrid.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `to_email` – Recipient's email address *(required)*
    - `subject` – Email subject line *(required)*
    - `message` – Email body content *(required)*

    <Tip>
      Use a verified sender email in SendGrid for better deliverability!
    </Tip>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Solar Savings (US Only)" icon="solar-panel">
    Calculate estimated savings from switching to solar based on monthly electricity bill and address.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `monthly_bill` – Current monthly electricity bill in USD *(required)*
    - `address` – Customer's full address *(required)*

    <Warning>
      **US Only:** This tool uses US solar data and pricing. Not accurate for other countries.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="/images/gohighlevel.png"
    alt="GoHighLevel"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>GoHighLevel Integration</h2>
</div>

Tools for integrating with your GoHighLevel CRM and calendars.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Find Or Create Contact" icon="user-plus">
    Find or create a contact in GoHighLevel to use for appointment booking and other functions.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `name` – The full name of the user *(optional)*
    - `phone` – Phone number in international format *(optional)*
    - `email` – Email address *(optional)*

    <Tip>
      Best practice: Use this tool at the start of your conversation flow to get the contact ID, then pass that ID to other GHL tools.
    </Tip>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Free Slots" icon="calendar-days">
    Fetch a list of available appointment slots for a GoHighLevel calendar within a specific time range.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `start_date` – Start date to search from in ISO 8601 format *(required)*
    - `end_date` – End date to search until in ISO 8601 format *(optional)*
    - `timezone` – Timezone in IANA format *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Booked Appointments" icon="calendar-check">
    Retrieve a list of appointments already booked for a specific contact.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `timezone` – Timezone in IANA format *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Cancel or Reschedule Appointment" icon="calendar-xmark">
    Cancel or reschedule a specific GoHighLevel appointment to a later date.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `action` – Either "cancel" or "reschedule" *(required)*
    - `appointment_id` – The ID of the appointment to modify *(required)*
    - `booking_id` – The booking ID *(required)*
    - `new_start_time` – New time in ISO8601 format *(required for reschedule)*
    - `timezone` – Timezone in IANA format *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Cal.com Integration</h2>
</div>

Tools for managing appointments with Cal.com calendars.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Fetch Free Slots" icon="calendar-days">
    Fetch available appointment slots between two dates for a specific Cal.com event type.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `start_date` – Start date to search from in ISO 8601 format *(required)*
    - `end_date` – End date to search until in ISO 8601 format *(optional)*
    - `timezone` – Timezone in IANA format *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get User Bookings" icon="calendar-check">
    Get a list of bookings for a specific user so you can reschedule or cancel them.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `attendee_email` – Email of the attendee *(required)*
    - `timezone` – Timezone in IANA format *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Cancel or Reschedule Booking" icon="calendar-xmark">
    Cancel or reschedule a booking made in Cal.com.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `action` – Either "cancel" or "reschedule" *(required)*
    - `booking_id` – The ID of the booking to modify *(required)*
    - `new_start_time` – New time in ISO8601 format *(required for reschedule)*
    - `timezone` – Timezone in IANA format *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

---

# MCP Application Integrations

Connect to 60+ popular applications through MCP application integrations. These applications are available as preset MCP servers—simply authenticate and select which tools you want your agent to access.

<Tip>
  **How it works:** When you add an MCP application integration, you'll
  authenticate your account and then choose specific tools/actions from that
  application. Your agent can then perform those actions during conversations.
  See the [MCP Server section](/chat-agents#mcp-server) for detailed setup
  instructions.
</Tip>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-acculynx.com"
    alt="AccuLynx"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>AccuLynx</h2>
</div>

Using the AccuLynx API, data can be seamlessly exchanged between AccuLynx and other applications for greater efficiency and productivity.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Add Job Appointment" icon="calendar-plus">
    Schedule the initial appointment for a specific job in the AccuLynx system.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `job_id` – The job ID for the appointment *(required)*
    - `start_date_time` – Start date and time for the appointment *(required)*
    - `end_date_time` – End date and time for the appointment *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Contact" icon="user-plus">
    Create a new contact in the AccuLynx system with detailed information.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - Contact details including name, phone, email, address, and other relevant information *(varies by field)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Job" icon="hammer">
    Create a new job in the AccuLynx system with the provided details.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` – The associated contact ID *(required)*
    - `location_address` – Location address for the job *(required)*
    - `job_category` – Category of the job *(optional)*
    - `work_type` – Type of work to be performed *(optional)*
    - `priority` – Job priority level *(optional)*
    - `trade_types` – Types of trades involved *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Lead" icon="lightbulb">
    Create a new lead in the AccuLynx system for residential roofing projects.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - Contact information for the lead *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Job Appointment Summary" icon="calendar-check">
    Retrieve a list of appointments from the calendar associated with a specific job.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `job_id` – The job ID to retrieve appointments for *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Of Calendars For The Location" icon="calendar-days">
    Retrieve a list of calendars associated with the authenticated user or organization.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None—returns all available calendars*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Of Contact Types Related To The Company" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of all available contact types in the AccuLynx system.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None—returns all contact types*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Company Representative" icon="user-gear">
    Add a company representative to a specific job within the AccuLynx system.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `job_id` – The job's unique identifier *(required)*
    - `representative_id` – The representative's ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>ActiveCampaign</h2>
</div>

ActiveCampaign is a marketing automation and CRM platform enabling businesses to manage email campaigns, sales pipelines, and customer segmentation to boost engagement and drive growth.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Add Contact Note" icon="note-sticky">
    Add a note to a contact in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Contact's email address *(required)*
    - `note` – The note content to add *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Contact To Automation" icon="robot">
    Add an existing contact to a specific automation in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Contact's email address *(required)*
    - `automation_id` – The automation ID to add the contact to *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Secondary Contact To Deal" icon="user-group">
    Add a secondary contact to an existing deal in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID to add *(required)*
    - `deal_id` – The deal ID *(required)*
    - `role_id` – The role ID for the contact *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Account" icon="building">
    Create a new account in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `account_name` – Name of the account *(required)*
    - `account_url` – Website URL of the account *(optional)*
    - `owner` – Account owner ID *(optional)*
    - Custom fields as needed *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Contact" icon="user-plus">
    Create a new contact in ActiveCampaign with the specified details.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Contact's email address *(required)*
    - `first_name` – Contact's first name *(optional)*
    - `last_name` – Contact's last name *(optional)*
    - `phone` – Contact's phone number *(optional)*
    - `organization` – Organization name *(optional)*
    - `tags` – Tags to apply to the contact *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Contact Task" icon="list-check">
    Create a task associated with a contact in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID *(required)*
    - `title` – Task title *(required)*
    - `description` – Task description *(optional)*
    - `due_date` – Task due date *(optional)*
    - `user_id` – User to assign the task to *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Deal Pipeline" icon="diagram-project">
    Create a new deal pipeline in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `pipeline_name` – Name of the pipeline *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Deal Task Type" icon="tags">
    Create a new deal task type in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_type_name` – Name of the task type *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Account" icon="trash">
    Delete an existing account in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `account_id` – The account ID to delete *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Deal Pipeline" icon="trash">
    Delete an existing deal pipeline in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `pipeline_id` – The pipeline ID to delete *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Deal Stage" icon="trash">
    Delete an existing deal stage in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `stage_id` – The stage ID to delete *(required)*
    - `type` – Either 'Move' or 'Delete' *(required)*
    - `new_pipeline_id` – New pipeline ID if type is 'Move' *(required if moving)*
    - `new_stage_id` – New stage ID if type is 'Move' *(required if moving)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Find Contact" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Find a specific contact in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Contact's email address *(optional)*
    - `contact_id` – Contact ID *(optional)*
    - `phone` – Contact's phone number *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Find Contact Task" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Find tasks associated with a specific contact in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID to search tasks for *(optional)*
    - `task_title` – Title of the task to find *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List All Contacts" icon="users">
    List all contacts in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `search` – Search term for name, organization, phone, or email *(optional)*
    - `email_like` – Email pattern to filter by *(optional)*
    - `list_id` – Filter by list ID *(optional)*
    - `tag_id` – Filter by tag ID *(optional)*
    - `segment_id` – Filter by segment ID *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `offset` – Pagination offset *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Manage Contact Tag" icon="tag">
    Manage tags for a contact in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` or `email` – Contact identifier *(required)*
    - `tag_name` – Name of the tag *(required)*
    - `action` – Either 'add' or 'remove' *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Manage List Subscription" icon="envelope-open">
    Subscribe or unsubscribe a contact from a list in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` or `email` – Contact identifier *(required)*
    - `list_id` – The list ID *(required)*
    - `action` – Either 'subscribe' or 'unsubscribe' *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Remove Contact From Automation" icon="user-xmark">
    Remove a contact from a specified automation in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Contact's email address *(required)*
    - `automation_id` – The automation ID to remove from *(required)*
    - `run_remove_option` – Remove from all runs or just latest *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Track Event" icon="chart-line">
    Create a custom website or application event in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_key` – Event key for authentication *(required)*
    - `event_actid` – Account ID *(required)*
    - `event_name` – Name of the event *(required)*
    - `event_value` – Event value *(optional)*
    - `event_contact_email` – Contact email associated with event *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Account" icon="pen">
    Update an existing account in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `account_id` – The account ID to update *(required)*
    - `account_name` – Updated account name *(optional)*
    - `account_url` – Updated website URL *(optional)*
    - Custom fields as needed *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Upsert Account" icon="arrows-rotate">
    Create a new account if it doesn't exist or update an existing account in ActiveCampaign.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `account_name` – Name of the account *(required)*
    - `account_url` – Website URL of the account *(optional)*
    - `owner` – Account owner ID *(optional)*
    - Custom fields as needed *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-airtable.com"
    alt="Airtable"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Airtable</h2>
</div>

Airtable merges spreadsheet functionality with database power, enabling teams to organize projects, track tasks, and collaborate through customizable views, automation, and integrations for data management.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Create Base" icon="database">
    Create a new Airtable base with specified tables and fields.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `workspace_id` – The workspace ID to create the base in *(required)*
    - `base_name` – Name of the base *(required)*
    - `tables` – Table definitions with fields *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Comment" icon="comment">
    Create a comment on a record in Airtable.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `base_id` – The base ID *(required)*
    - `table_id_or_name` – The table ID or name *(required)*
    - `record_id` – The record ID to comment on *(required)*
    - `comment_text` – The comment content *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Field" icon="plus">
    Create a new field in an Airtable table.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `base_id` – The base ID *(required)*
    - `table_id_or_name` – The table ID or name *(required)*
    - `field_name` – Name of the new field *(required)*
    - `field_type` – Type of field (text, number, date, etc.) *(required)*
    - Field options based on type *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Multiple Records" icon="list-plus">
    Create multiple records in an Airtable table.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `base_id` – The base ID *(required)*
    - `table_id_or_name` – The table ID or name *(required)*
    - `records` – Array of record objects with field values *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Record" icon="plus">
    Create a new record in an Airtable table.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `base_id` – The base ID *(required)*
    - `table_id_or_name` – The table ID or name *(required)*
    - `fields` – Object with field names and values *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Table" icon="table">
    Create a new table in an Airtable base.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `base_id` – The base ID *(required)*
    - `table_name` – Name of the new table *(required)*
    - `description` – Table description *(optional)*
    - `fields` – Field definitions for the table *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Comment" icon="trash">
    Delete a comment from a record in Airtable.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `base_id` – The base ID *(required)*
    - `table_id_or_name` – The table ID or name *(required)*
    - `record_id` – The record ID *(required)*
    - `comment_id` – The comment ID to delete *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Multiple Records" icon="trash">
    Delete multiple records from an Airtable table.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `base_id` – The base ID *(required)*
    - `table_id_or_name` – The table ID or name *(required)*
    - `record_ids` – Array of record IDs to delete (max 10) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Record" icon="trash">
    Delete a record from an Airtable table.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `base_id` – The base ID *(required)*
    - `table_id_or_name` – The table ID or name *(required)*
    - `record_id` – The record ID to delete *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  </Accordion>

<AccordionGroup>

    - `followers` – Array of user GIDs to add as followers *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Task To Section" icon="list">
    Add a task to a section in Asana.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_gid` – The task GID *(required)*
    - `section_gid` – The section GID *(required)*
    - `insert_before` – Task GID to insert before *(optional)*
    - `insert_after` – Task GID to insert after *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Project" icon="folder-plus">

    - `workspace` or `team` – Workspace or team GID *(required)*
    - Project details (notes, color, etc.) *(optional)*

    - `name` – Tag name *(required)*
    - `color` – Tag color *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Task" icon="plus">
    Create a new task in Asana.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `name` – Task name *(required)*
    - `workspace` or `parent` or `projects` – Association (workspace, parent task, or projects) *(required)*
    - `notes` – Task description *(optional)*
    - `due_on` or `due_at` – Due date *(optional)*
    - `assignee` – Assignee user GID *(optional)*
    - `followers` – Array of follower GIDs *(optional)*
    - `projects` – Array of project GIDs *(optional)*
    - `tags` – Array of tag GIDs *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Custom Field" icon="list">

  </Accordion>

  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>BambooHR</h2>
</div>

BambooHR is an American technology company that provides human resources software as a service.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Add A Benefit Group Employee" icon="user-plus">
    Associate an employee with a benefit group in BambooHR.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `employee_id` – The employee ID *(required)*
    - `benefit_group_id` – The benefit group ID *(required)*

    - `end_date` – End date for enrollment *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  </Accordion>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/brevo.svg"
    alt="Brevo"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Brevo</h2>
</div>

Brevo is an all-in-one marketing platform that helps businesses grow through email marketing, SMS, chat, and CRM tools.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Create A Company" icon="building">
    Create a new company in your Brevo account.

    **Description:**
    This tool allows you to create a new company in your Brevo account.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - Company information (name, industry, etc.) *(required)*
    - Additional company attributes *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Company" icon="trash">
    Delete a company from Brevo.

    **Description:**
    Deletes a company from Brevo using its unique identifier.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `company_id` – The company ID to delete *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Contact" icon="trash">
    Delete a contact from Brevo.

    **Description:**
    Deletes a contact from Brevo using its unique identifier.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID to delete *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Find Contact" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Check if a contact exists in Brevo.

    **Description:**
    This tool checks if a contact exists in Brevo. It searches for a contact using either an email address or mobile number, with the email being prioritized if both are provided.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Contact's email address *(optional)*
    - `mobile` – Contact's mobile number *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get All Contacts" icon="users">
    Retrieve all contacts from your Brevo account.

    **Description:**
    This tool retrieves all contacts from your Brevo account. It allows for pagination and filtering based on modification/creation dates, list IDs, segment IDs, and contact attributes.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of contacts to retrieve *(optional)*
    - `offset` – Pagination offset *(optional)*
    - `modified_since` – Filter by modification date *(optional)*
    - `created_since` – Filter by creation date *(optional)*
    - `list_id` – Filter by list ID *(optional)*
    - `segment_id` – Filter by segment ID *(optional)*
    - Attribute filters *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Company Details" icon="building">
    Retrieve details of a specific company.

    **Description:**
    This tool retrieves the details of a specific company by its unique ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `company_id` – The company ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Contact Details" icon="user">
    Retrieve detailed information about a specific contact.

    **Description:**
    This tool retrieves detailed information about a specific contact in Brevo. You can identify the contact using their email address (URL-encoded), their unique contact ID, or their SMS attribute value.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Contact's email address *(optional)*
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID *(optional)*
    - `sms` – SMS attribute value *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List All Companies" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of all companies in Brevo CRM.

    **Description:**
    This action retrieves a list of all companies stored in the Brevo CRM. It supports pagination and filtering by name and other attributes.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of companies to retrieve *(optional)*
    - `offset` – Pagination offset *(optional)*
    - `name` – Filter by company name *(optional)*
    - Attribute filters *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-bill.com"
    alt="BILL"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>BILL</h2>
</div>

BILL is a leading provider of cloud-based software that simplifies, digitizes, and automates back-office financial processes for small and mid-sized businesses. Our customers come from all industries, ranging from startups to established brands and nonprofits to franchises.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Accept Network Invitation" icon="user-check">
    Accept a network invitation that was sent to the organization by a vendor or customer. When the invitation is accepted, the organization is connected with the vendor or customer in the BILL network. See [BILL network](doc:bill-network) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Approve Or Deny A Reimbursement" icon="check-circle">
    Approve or deny a reimbursement.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Archive A Bill" icon="archive">
    Archive an existing bill. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `true`. You can restore an archived bill with `POST /v3/bills/{billId}/restore`. There is no change when you archive an archived bill.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Archive A Customer" icon="archive">
    Archive an existing customer. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `true`. You can restore an archived customer with `POST /v3/customers/{customerId}/restore`. There is no change when you archive an archived customer.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Archive An Invoice" icon="archive">
    Archive an existing invoice. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `true`. You can restore an archived invoice with `POST /v3/invoices/{invoiceId}/restore`. There is no change when you archive an archived invoice.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Archive An Item" icon="archive">
    Archive an existing item. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `true`.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Archive A Recurring Bill" icon="archive">
    Archive a recurring bill. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `true`. You can restore an archived recurring bill with `POST /v3/recurringbills/{recurringbillId}/restore`. There is no change when you archive an archived recurring bill. When a recurring bill is modified, all future bills are automatically changed.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Archive A Vendor" icon="archive">
    Archive an existing vendor. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `true`. You can restore an archived vendor with `POST /v3/vendors/{vendorId}/restore`. There is no change when you archive an archived vendor.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Cancel A Payment" icon="xmark-circle">
    Cancel an existing payment. You can attempt to cancel a payment with `POST /v3/payments/{paymentId}/cancel` based on a set of conditions. See <a href="https://help.bill.com/hc/en-us/articles/115005898063">Payment cancelation and void cut-off timing</a> in the BILL Help Center to learn about the BILL cancel payment process and timing. If the conditions are not met, you cannot cancel the payment. At that point, you can attempt to void the payment with `POST /v3/payments/{paymentId}/void`.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Bank Account" icon="building-columns">
    Create a new bank account. The currently signed-in user must have the `ADMINISTRATOR` user role in the BILL organization to perform this operation. BILL sends an email notification for informing you about changes to your funding accounts. **Note**: When you create a bank account, BILL sends a test ACH payment to the bank account to confirm whether the account details are accurate. In the response, three fields are set to their default values. * The bank account `status` is set as `PENDING`. You can verify t

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Bill" icon="file-invoice">
    Create a new bill. See [Bills](doc:ap-bills) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Customer" icon="user-plus">
    Create a new customer. See [Customers](doc:ar-customers) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create An Invoice" icon="file-invoice-dollar">
    Create a new invoice. See [Invoices](doc:ar-invoices) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create An Item" icon="plus-circle">
    Create a new item.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Payment" icon="credit-card">
    Create a payment. See [Get list of vendor payment options](ref:listpaymentoptions) to get details about vendor payment options and payment process dates. **Note**: Creating a payment requires an MFA-trusted API session. See [MFA setup](ref:setup) for information about the BILL MFA process. See [Payments](doc:ap-payments) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Recurring Bill" icon="repeat">
    Create a recurring bill. See [Recurring bills](doc:ap-recurring-bills) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Reimbursement" icon="receipt">
    Create a reimbursement

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Vendor" icon="store">
    Creates a new vendor in the Bill.com system with comprehensive details for invoicing and payment processing. This endpoint allows you to set up a vendor's basic information, address, payment preferences, tax details, and auto-pay settings. It's particularly useful when onboarding new suppliers or updating existing vendor information en masse. The endpoint requires at minimum the vendor's name and address, but allows for extensive customization of payment terms, currencies, and automated payment rules.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Vendor Bank Account" icon="building-columns">
    Create a vendor bank account for an existing vendor. To update vendor bank account information, you must first delete the existing vendor bank account (with `DELETE /v3/vendors/{vendorId}/bank-account`), and then create a new vendor bank account (with `POST /v3/vendors/{vendorId}/bank-account`) with the updated information. **Note**: When you add vendor bank account information, BILL requires 2 business days to complete a one-time verification of the bank account.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete A Reimbursement" icon="trash">
    Delete a specified reimbursement.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete A Vendor Bank Account" icon="trash">
    Delete the existing vendor bank account for a vendor. To update vendor bank account information, you must first delete the existing vendor bank account (with `DELETE /v3/vendors/{vendorId}/bank-account`), and then create a new vendor bank account (with `POST /v3/vendors/{vendorId}/bank-account`) with the updated information.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Customer Connection" icon="link-slash">
    Delete an existing network connection with a customer. In addition, use this endpoint to cancel a pending customer connection invite. You can send a new connection invitation after an existing connection or invitation is canceled. **Note**: If the invited customer does not respond to an invitation for 60 days, the invitation expires. See [BILL network](doc:bill-network) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Vendor Connection" icon="link-slash">
    Delete an existing network connection with a vendor. In addition, use this endpoint to cancel a pending vendor connection invite. You can send a new connection invitation after an existing connection or invitation is canceled. **Note**: If the invited vendor does not respond to an invitation for 60 days, the invitation expires. See [BILL network](doc:bill-network) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Bank Account Details" icon="building-columns">
    Get details about an existing bank account.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Bill Details" icon="file-invoice">
    Get details about an existing bill.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Card Funding Purpose" icon="credit-card">
    Get a list of card funding purpose values based on the vendor and card brand. When you create a payment (`POST /v3/payments` or `POST /v3/payments/bulk`) with a `CARD_ACCOUNT` funding account `type`, BILL requires a vendor industry value for compliance. When BILL cannot identify the vendor industry, the `cardFundingPurpose` field must be set in your payment request. Use this endpoint to get the list of card funding purpose values you can set.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Check Image Data" icon="image">
    Get images of an existing check sent to a vendor. From the response, use `downloadLink` in a GET request to download the front and back images of the check. ``` curl '{downloadLink}&sessionId={session_id}' --output {check_name} ```

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Customer Details" icon="user">
    Get details about an existing customer.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Customer Invitation Status" icon="envelope-open">
    Get the status of an existing invitation sent with `POST /v3/network/invitation/customer/{customerId}`. When the customer accepts the invitation, your organization is connected with the customer. **Note**: If the invited customer does not respond to an invitation for 60 days, the invitation expires. See [BILL network](doc:bill-network) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get International Payments Configuration" icon="globe">
    Get international payments (not USD) configuration that is required for compliance with international payment rules of a vendor country and vendor bank account. This information is based on vendor country, bill currency, and vendor account type. Use this endpoint for getting information before creating an international vendor. In the response, the required `paymentPurpose` and `regulatoryFields` information is retrieved for the vendor.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Invoice Details" icon="file-invoice-dollar">
    Get details about an existing invoice.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Item Details" icon="box">
    Get details about an existing item.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Of Bank Accounts" icon="list">
    Get a list of bank account objects. By default, you get 20 results on one page of results. Set `max` in your request to get up to 100 results on one page. See [Search operations with lists](doc:search-op-with-lists) in the Guides section for filtering, sorting, and pagination examples.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Of Bills" icon="list">

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Of Customers" icon="list">
    Get a list of customer objects. By default, you get 20 results on one page of results. Set `max` in your request to get up to 100 results on one page. See [Search operations with lists](doc:search-op-with-lists) in the Guides section for filtering, sorting, and pagination examples.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Of Invoices" icon="list">

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Of Items" icon="list">

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Of Payments" icon="list">

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Of Recurring Bills" icon="list">
    Get a list of recurring bill objects. By default, you get 20 results on one page of results. Set `max` in your request to get up to 100 results on one page. See [Search operations with lists](doc:search-op-with-lists) in the Guides section for filtering, sorting, and pagination examples.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Of Reimbursements" icon="list">
    Get a list of reimbursement objects.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Of Transactions" icon="list">
    Get a list of transaction objects.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Of Vendor Payment Options" icon="list">
    Get a list of vendor payment options available based on the funding account options available in the signed-in user's BILL organization and on the payment methods accepted by a vendor. See [Vendor payment options](doc:vendor-payment-options) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Of Vendors" icon="list">
    Get a list of vendor objects. By default, you get 20 results on one page of results. Set `max` in your request to get up to 100 results on one page. See [Search operations with lists](doc:search-op-with-lists) in the Guides section for filtering, sorting, and pagination examples.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Payment Details" icon="credit-card">

    Get details about an existing transaction.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Vendor Bank Account Details" icon="building-columns">
    Get details about an existing vendor bank account.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Vendor Configuration" icon="cog">
    Get international payments (not USD) configuration after vendor creation. This configuration is required for compliance with international payment rules of a vendor country and vendor bank account. In the response, the required `paymentPurpose` and `regulatoryFields` information is retrieved for the vendor.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Vendor Details" icon="store">
    Get details about an existing vendor.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Vendor Invitation Status" icon="envelope-open">
    Get the status of an existing invitation sent with `POST /v3/network/invitation/vendor/{vendorId}`. When the vendor accepts the invitation, your organization is connected with the vendor. **Note**: If the invited vendor does not respond to an invitation for 60 days, the invitation expires. See [BILL network](doc:bill-network) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Invite A Customer In The Bill Network" icon="envelope">
    Send an invitation to connect a customer created in your organization with a customer in the network. BILL sends an invitation email to the customer email address. When the customer accepts the invitation, the customer in your organization is connected with the invited customer. If the invited customer does not respond, delete the invitation (with `DELETE /v3/network/invitation/customer/{customerId}`) before sending a new invitation.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Invite A Vendor In The Bill Network" icon="envelope">
    Send an invitation to connect a vendor created in your organization with a vendor in the network. BILL sends an invitation email to the vendor email address. When the vendor accepts the invitation, the vendor in your organization is connected with the invited vendor. If the invited vendor does not respond, delete the invitation (with `DELETE /v3/network/invitation/vendor/{vendorId}`) before sending a new invitation.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Record Ar Payment" icon="money-bill-wave">
    Record an invoice payment received outside your BILL system. Apply the recorded payment amount to one or more invoices for a customer. Any recorded unapplied amount is an overpayment and is available as a customer balance in your BILL system. See [Recording an AR payment](doc:recording-an-ar-payment) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Replace A Bill" icon="edit">
    Update the number of line items in a bill. You can also update other bill details. You can use the PUT operation to add, remove, or replace the number of line items in a bill. A set of rules apply with the PUT operation. * When you add a new line item, a new line item `id` is generated in the bill. * When you omit an existing line item `id`, the line item is removed from the bill.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Replace An Invoice" icon="edit">
    Update the number of line items in an invoice. You can also update other invoice details. You can use the PUT operation to add, remove, or replace the number of line items in an invoice. A set of rules apply with the PUT operation. * When you add a new line item, a new line item `id` is generated in the invoice. * When you omit an existing line item `id`, the line item is removed from the invoice.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Replace A Recurring Bill" icon="edit">
    Update the number of line items in a recurring bill. You can also update other recurring bill details. You can use the PUT operation to add, remove, or replace the number of line items in a recurring bill. A set of rules apply with the PUT operation. * When you add a new line item, a new line item `id` is generated in the bill. * When you omit an existing line item `id`, the line item is removed from the bill. When a recurring bill is modified, all future bills are automatically changed.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Restore An Archived Bill" icon="rotate-left">
    Restore an archived bill. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `false`. You can perform any valid BILL operation on restored bills. There is no change when you restore a restored bill.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Restore An Archived Customer" icon="rotate-left">
    Restore an archived customer. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `false`. You can perform any valid BILL operation on restored customers. There is no change when you restore a restored customer.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Restore An Archived Invoice" icon="rotate-left">
    Restore an archived invoice. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `false`. You can perform any valid BILL operation on restored invoices. There is no change when you restore a restored invoice.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Restore An Archived Item" icon="rotate-left">
    Restore an archived item. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `false`.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Restore An Archived Recurring Bill" icon="rotate-left">
    Restore an archived recurring bill. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `false`. You can perform any valid BILL operation on restored recurring bills. There is no change when you restore a restored recurring bill. When a recurring bill is modified, all future bills are automatically changed.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Restore An Archived Vendor" icon="rotate-left">
    Restore an archived vendor. In the response, the `archived` field is set as `false`. You can perform any valid BILL operation on restored vendors. There is no change when you restore a restored vendor.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Search For An Organization In The Bill Networks" icon="search">
    Search for a customer, vendor, or verified national vendor. You can search in the BILL network and verified national vendor network. When you search in the BILL network, there are two `name` requirements for getting search results. * Your search term must have a minimum of three characters. * Your search term must be a complete word. You will not get search results when your search term is a partial word.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Send An Invoice" icon="paper-plane">
    Send an invoice to a customer email address. You can send the invoice to multiple email addresses. See [Invoices](doc:ar-invoices) in the Guides section for more information, sample requests, and responses.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update A Bank Account" icon="edit">
    Update details about an existing bank account. This operation follows a set of rules. * **Bank account `status` requirement**: The bank account `status` must be set as `VERIFIED` before you can update any details about the bank account. You can verify the bank account with `POST /v3/funding-accounts/banks/{bankAccountId}/verify`. * **Update field restrictions**: You cannot update the `routingNumber`, `accountNumber`, and account `type` values for a bank account. If you want to update any of these values, cr

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update A Bill" icon="edit">
    Update details about a bill line item. You can also update other bill details. You can use the PATCH operation to modify line item details, such as `amount` and `description`. The bill line item `id` does not change with a PATCH operation.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update A Customer" icon="edit">
    Update details about an existing customer.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update An Invoice" icon="edit">
    Update details about an invoice line item. You can also update other invoice details. You can use the PATCH operation to modify line item details, such as `amount`, `quantity`, and `description`. The invoice line item `id` does not change with a PATCH operation.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update An Item" icon="edit">
    Update details about an existing item.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update A Recurring Bill" icon="edit">
    Update details about a recurring bill line item. You can also update other recurring bill details. You can use the PATCH operation to modify line item details, such as amount and description. The recurring bill line item `id` does not change with a PATCH operation. When a recurring bill is modified, all future bills are automatically changed.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update A Reimbursement" icon="edit">
    Update a reimbursement

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update A Vendor" icon="edit">
    Update details about an existing vendor. ### Requirements for enabling vendor payments Vendor address details are required for paying a vendor by check or for inviting the vendor to join the BILL network. * `line1` * `city` * `zipOrPostalCode` * `country` * `payeeName` **Note**: You cannot add or update vendor bank account information with this endpoint. You can add and manage vendor bank account information with a dedicated set of endpoints.

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Transaction" icon="edit">
    Update a transaction

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Void A Payment" icon="ban">
    Void an existing payment. Void a bill payment that has started processing and cannot be canceled (with `POST /v3/payments/{paymentId}/cancel`). You can attempt to void payments made both with BILL (online) and outside BILL (offline). ### Void a payment made with BILL (online) In your /`POST /v3/payments/{paymentId}/void` request: * Set `paymentId` as the BILL-generated ID of the payment. The value begins with `stp`.

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/cal_vC2IAGj.com_N0Xu85Y.png"
    alt="Cal.com"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Cal.com</h2>
</div>

Cal simplifies meeting coordination by providing shareable booking pages, calendar syncing, and availability management to streamline the scheduling process.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Cancel Booking Via Uid" icon="calendar-xmark">
    Cancel an existing booking in Cal.com.

    **Description:**
    Cancels an existing and active Cal.com booking using its unique identifier (UID).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `booking_uid` – The booking UID to cancel *(required)*
    - `reason` – Reason for cancellation *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Check Calendar Version2" icon="calendar-check">
    Check calendar availability.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves free/busy availability for a specified calendar to aid scheduling without revealing event details; requires an existing, accessible calendar, noting that data granularity can vary.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The calendar ID to check *(required)*
    - `start_date` – Start date for availability check *(required)*
    - `end_date` – End date for availability check *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Phone Call Event" icon="phone">
    Schedule a phone call event in Cal.com.

    **Description:**
    Schedules a phone call event in Cal.com using existing eventType, organization, and team IDs; this action only registers the event details and does not initiate the actual phone call.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_type_id` – The event type ID *(required)*
    - `organization_id` – The organization ID *(optional)*
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(optional)*
    - `start_time` – Event start time *(required)*
    - `attendee_email` – Attendee email address *(required)*
    - `attendee_name` – Attendee name *(required)*
    - `phone_number` – Phone number for the call *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch All Bookings" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of bookings.

    **Description:**
    Fetches a list of bookings, optionally filtered by status, attendee, date range, or by event/team IDs (which must belong to/include the authenticated user respectively), with support for pagination and sorting.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `status` – Filter by booking status *(optional)*
    - `attendee_email` – Filter by attendee email *(optional)*
    - `start_date` – Filter by start date *(optional)*
    - `end_date` – Filter by end date *(optional)*
    - `event_type_id` – Filter by event type ID *(optional)*
    - `team_id` – Filter by team ID *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `offset` – Pagination offset *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Event Types" icon="list">
    Retrieve Cal.com event types.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves Cal event types, filterable by `username` (required if `eventSlug` is provided), multiple `usernames`, or organization details (`orgSlug` or `orgId`).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `username` – Filter by username *(optional)*
    - `event_slug` – Filter by event slug (requires username) *(optional)*
    - `usernames` – Filter by multiple usernames *(optional)*
    - `org_slug` – Filter by organization slug *(optional)*
    - `org_id` – Filter by organization ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Post New Booking Request" icon="calendar-plus">
    Create a new booking in Cal.com.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new booking for an active event type, scheduling it for a specified start time (preferably in the future) with primary attendee details and optional customizations.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_type_id` – The event type ID *(required)*
    - `start_time` – Booking start time *(required)*
    - `attendee_email` – Primary attendee email *(required)*
    - `attendee_name` – Primary attendee name *(required)*
    - `timezone` – Timezone for the booking *(optional)*
    - `notes` – Booking notes *(optional)*
    - `metadata` – Additional metadata *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Reschedule Booking By Uid" icon="calendar">
    Reschedule an existing booking.

    **Description:**
    Reschedules an existing booking (identified by `bookingUid`) to a new time, provided the new slot's availability is confirmed beforehand; all other rescheduling parameters (e.g., new date, time) must be sent in the POST request body, not via this action's direct parameters.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `booking_uid` – The booking UID to reschedule *(required)*
    - `new_start_time` – New start time for the booking *(required)*
    - `timezone` – Timezone for the new time *(optional)*
    - `reschedule_reason` – Reason for rescheduling *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-calendarhero.com"
    alt="CalendarHero"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>CalendarHero</h2>
</div>

CalendarHero is a versatile scheduling tool designed to streamline and simplify your calendar management. It integrates seamlessly with your existing calendars, allowing you to efficiently schedule, reschedule, and manage meetings with ease.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Add Calendar Connection" icon="calendar-plus">
    Add a calendar integration to a user's account.

    **Description:**
    Tool to add a calendar integration to a user's account. Use after gathering provider credentials.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `provider` – Calendar provider (Google, Outlook, etc.) *(required)*
    - `credentials` – Provider credentials *(required)*
    - Additional provider-specific settings *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Contact" icon="user-plus">
    Create a new contact in CalendarHero.

    **Description:**
    Tool to create a new contact. Use after confirming contact details before making the API call.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `name` – Contact name *(required)*
    - `email` – Contact email address *(required)*
    - `phone` – Contact phone number *(optional)*
    - Additional contact details *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Meeting Request V2" icon="calendar-plus">
    Create a new meeting request in CalendarHero.

    **Description:**
    Tool to create a new meeting request in CalendarHero. Use when scheduling a meeting with participants, time range, and additional details.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `participants` – Array of participant emails *(required)*
    - `start_time` – Meeting start time *(required)*
    - `end_time` – Meeting end time *(required)*
    - `title` – Meeting title *(optional)*
    - `description` – Meeting description *(optional)*
    - `location` – Meeting location *(optional)*
    - `timezone` – Timezone for the meeting *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Contact" icon="user">
    Retrieve contact information.

    **Description:**
    Fetch Contact

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Meeting Details" icon="calendar">
    Fetch details for meetings within a timeframe.

    **Description:**
    Tool to fetch details for meetings within a specified timeframe. Use this after user provides start and end datetimes in ISO8601.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `start_time` – Start datetime in ISO8601 format *(required)*
    - `end_time` – End datetime in ISO8601 format *(required)*
    - `meeting_id` – Specific meeting ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Meetings" icon="list">
    Retrieve meetings within a timeframe.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve the user's meetings within a specified timeframe. Use after confirming date range to fetch raw calendar data.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `start_time` – Start datetime *(required)*
    - `end_time` – End datetime *(required)*
    - `calendar_id` – Filter by calendar ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Meeting Templates" icon="list">
    List all available meeting templates.

    **Description:**
    Tool to list all meeting templates available for quick scheduling. Use after authenticating and when you need to retrieve available templates before scheduling.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None—returns all available templates*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Meeting Types" icon="list">
    Retrieve user's configured meeting types.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve the user's configured meeting types. Use after authenticating with CalendarHero.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None—returns all meeting types*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List User Calendars" icon="calendar">
    List all calendar integrations for a user.

    **Description:**
    Tool to list all calendar integrations connected to a user's CalendarHero account. Use after authenticating when you need to retrieve available calendars for scheduling.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None—returns all connected calendars*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Search Contact" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Search for existing contacts.

    **Description:**
    Tool to search for existing contacts. Use after confirming a need to find contacts by email or name.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Search by email address *(optional)*
    - `name` – Search by name *(optional)*
    - `query` – General search query *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Send Reminder" icon="bell">
    Send a reminder to a contact about their meeting.

    **Description:**
    Tool to send a reminder to a contact about their scheduled meeting. Use after confirming the meeting task ID to notify participants.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `meeting_task_id` – The meeting task ID *(required)*
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID to send reminder to *(required)*
    - `message` – Custom reminder message *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Contact" icon="pen">
    Update details of an existing contact.

    **Description:**
    Tool to update details of an existing contact. Use when you have the contact's ID and want to apply changes. Example: 'Update contact 507f1f77bcf86cd799439011 with a new email.'

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID to update *(required)*
    - Updated contact fields (name, email, phone, etc.) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/calendly.svg"
    alt="Calendly"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Calendly</h2>
</div>

Calendly is an appointment scheduling tool that automates meeting invitations, availability checks, and reminders, helping individuals and teams avoid email back-and-forth.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Cancel Event" icon="calendar-xmark">
    Cancel an existing scheduled event.

    **Description:**
    Permanently cancels an existing, active scheduled event by its `uuid`, optionally providing a `reason`, which may trigger notifications to invitees.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_uuid` – The event UUID to cancel *(required)*
    - `reason` – Reason for cancellation *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Invitee No Show" icon="user-xmark">
    Mark an invitee as a no-show.

    **Description:**
    Marks an Invitee, identified by their existing and valid URI, as a "No Show" for a scheduled event.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `invitee_uri` – The invitee URI *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create One Off Event Type" icon="calendar-plus">
    Create a temporary one-off event type.

    **Description:**
    Creates a temporary Calendly one-off event type for unique meetings outside regular availability, requiring valid host/co-host URIs, a future date/range for `date_setting`, and a positive `duration`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `host_uri` – Host URI *(required)*
    - `co_host_uris` – Array of co-host URIs *(optional)*
    - `date_setting` – Date range settings *(required)*
    - `duration` – Event duration in minutes *(required)*
    - `name` – Event type name *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Scheduling Link" icon="link">
    Create a single-use scheduling link.

    **Description:**
    Create a single-use scheduling link. Creates a scheduling link that can be used to book an event. The link allows invitees to schedule up to the specified maximum number of events. Once the limit is reached, the link becomes inactive.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_type_uri` – The event type URI *(required)*
    - `max_booking_count` – Maximum number of bookings *(required)*
    - Additional link settings *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Share" icon="share">
    Create a customizable share link for an event type.

    **Description:**
    Creates a customizable, one-time share link for a Calendly event type, allowing specific overrides to its settings (e.g., duration, availability, location) without altering the original event type.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_type_uri` – The event type URI *(required)*
    - `duration` – Override duration *(optional)*
    - `availability` – Override availability *(optional)*
    - `location` – Override location *(optional)*
    - Additional override settings *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Single Use Scheduling Link" icon="link">
    Create a one-time scheduling link.

    **Description:**
    Creates a one-time, single-use scheduling link for an active Calendly event type, expiring after one booking.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_type_uri` – The event type URI *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Invitee No Show" icon="trash">
    Delete an invitee no-show record.

    **Description:**
    Deletes an Invitee No-Show record by its `uuid` to reverse an invitee's "no-show" status; the `uuid` must refer to an existing record.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `no_show_uuid` – The no-show record UUID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Scheduled Event Data" icon="trash">
    Delete scheduled event data (Enterprise only).

    **Description:**
    For Enterprise users, initiates deletion of an organization's scheduled event data between a `start_time` and `end_time` (inclusive, where `start_time` must be less than or equal to `end_time`); actual data deletion may take up to 7 days to complete.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `start_time` – Start time for deletion range *(required)*
    - `end_time` – End time for deletion range *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Current User" icon="user">
    Retrieve current authenticated user information.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information about the currently authenticated Calendly user.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None—returns current user information*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Event" icon="calendar">
    Retrieve a specific scheduled event.

    **Description:**
    Use to retrieve a specific Calendly scheduled event by its UUID, provided the event exists in the user's Calendly account.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_uuid` – The event UUID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Event Invitee" icon="user">
    Retrieve invitee information for an event.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information about a specific invitee of a scheduled event, using their unique UUIDs.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_uuid` – The event UUID *(required)*
    - `invitee_uuid` – The invitee UUID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Event Type" icon="calendar">
    Retrieve details for a specific event type.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves details for a specific Calendly event type, identified by its UUID, which must be valid and correspond to an existing event type.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_type_uuid` – The event type UUID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Invitee No Show" icon="user-xmark">
    Retrieve invitee no-show record details.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves details for a specific Invitee No Show record by its UUID; an Invitee No Show is marked when an invitee does not attend a scheduled event.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `no_show_uuid` – The no-show record UUID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get User" icon="user">
    Retrieve comprehensive user details.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves comprehensive details for an existing Calendly user.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user_uuid` – The user UUID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get User Availability Schedule" icon="calendar-check">
    Retrieve user availability schedule.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves an existing user availability schedule by its UUID; this schedule defines the user's default hours of availability.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `schedule_uuid` – The schedule UUID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Event Invitees" icon="users">
    Retrieve list of invitees for an event.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of invitees for a specified Calendly event UUID, with options to filter by status or email, and sort by creation time.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_uuid` – The event UUID *(required)*
    - `status` – Filter by invitee status *(optional)*
    - `email` – Filter by email address *(optional)*
    - `sort` – Sort order (creation_time) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Events" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of scheduled events.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of scheduled Calendly events; requires `user`, `organization`, `group`, or `invitee_email` for scope, and admin rights may be needed when filtering by `organization` or `group`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user` – Filter by user URI *(optional)*
    - `organization` – Filter by organization URI *(optional)*
    - `group` – Filter by group URI *(optional)*
    - `invitee_email` – Filter by invitee email *(optional)*
    - `count` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `page_token` – Pagination token *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Event Type Available Times" icon="clock">
    Fetch available time slots for an event type.

    **Description:**
    Fetches available time slots for a Calendly event type within a specified time range; results are not paginated.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_type_uri` – The event type URI *(required)*
    - `start_time` – Start time for availability check *(required)*
    - `end_time` – End time for availability check *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Event Type Hosts" icon="users">
    Retrieve hosts for an event type.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of hosts (users) assigned to a specific, existing Calendly event type, identified by its URI.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_type_uri` – The event type URI *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List User Busy Times" icon="calendar-xmark">
    Fetch user's busy time intervals.

    **Description:**
    Fetches a user's busy time intervals (internal and external calendar events) in ascending order for a period up to 7 days; keyset pagination is not supported.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user_uri` – The user URI *(required)*
    - `start_time` – Start time for busy check *(required)*
    - `end_time` – End time for busy check (max 7 days) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List User S Event Types" icon="list">
    Retrieve event types for a user or organization.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves event types for a user or organization; requires either the `user` or `organization` URI.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user` – Filter by user URI *(optional)*
    - `organization` – Filter by organization URI *(optional)*
    - `count` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `page_token` – Pagination token *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>
