<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/clickup.svg"
    alt="ClickUp"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>ClickUp</h2>
</div>

ClickUp unifies tasks, docs, goals, and chat in a single platform, allowing teams to plan, organize, and collaborate across projects with customizable workflows.

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Add Tag To Task" icon="tag">
    Add an existing tag to a task.

    **Description:**
    Adds an existing tag to a specified task; team_id is required if custom_task_ids is true.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `tag_name` – The tag name to add *(required)*
    - `team_id` – Team ID (required if custom_task_ids is true) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Task To List" icon="list">
    Add a task to an additional list.

    **Description:**
    Adds an existing task to an additional ClickUp List; the "Tasks in Multiple Lists" ClickApp must be enabled in the Workspace for this.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `list_id` – The list ID to add the task to *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create A Time Entry" icon="clock">
    Create a new time entry for a team.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new time entry for a specified team.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(optional)*
    - `start` – Start time *(required)*
    - `duration` – Duration in milliseconds *(required)*
    - `description` – Time entry description *(optional)*
    - `billable` – Whether the entry is billable *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Checklist" icon="list-check">
    Create a new checklist in a task.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new checklist with a specified name within an existing task, which can be identified by its standard ID or a custom task ID (if `custom_task_ids` is true, `team_id` is also required).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Checklist name *(required)*
    - `team_id` – Team ID (required if custom_task_ids is true) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Checklist Item" icon="list-check">
    Create a new checklist item.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new checklist item within a specified, existing checklist, optionally setting the item's name and assigning it to a user.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `checklist_id` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Item name *(required)*
    - `assignee` – User ID to assign to *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create List" icon="list">
    Create a new list in a folder.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new list in ClickUp within a specified, existing folder.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `folder_id` – The folder ID *(required)*
    - `name` – List name *(required)*
    - Additional list settings *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create List Comment" icon="comment">
    Add a comment to a list.

    **Description:**
    Adds a new comment with specific text to an existing and accessible ClickUp List, assigns it to a user, and sets notification preferences for all list members.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `list_id` – The list ID *(required)*
    - `comment_text` – Comment text *(required)*
    - `assignee` – User ID to assign comment to *(optional)*
    - `notify_all` – Notify all list members *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Task" icon="plus">
    Create a new task in a list.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new ClickUp task in a specific list, optionally as a subtask if a `parent` task ID (which cannot be a subtask itself and must be in the same list) is provided.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `list_id` – The list ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Task name *(required)*
    - `parent` – Parent task ID for subtasks *(optional)*
    - `description` – Task description *(optional)*
    - `assignees` – Array of assignee user IDs *(optional)*
    - `status` – Task status *(optional)*
    - `priority` – Task priority *(optional)*
    - `due_date` – Due date timestamp *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Task Comment" icon="comment">
    Add a comment to a task.

    **Description:**
    Adds a comment to a ClickUp task; `team_id` is required if `custom_task_ids` is true.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `comment_text` – Comment text *(required)*
    - `team_id` – Team ID (required if custom_task_ids is true) *(optional)*
    - `assignee` – User ID to assign comment to *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Task From Template" icon="file">
    Create a task from a template.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new task in a specified ClickUp list from a task template, using the provided name for the new task.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `list_id` – The list ID *(required)*
    - `template_id` – The template ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Task name *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete A Time Entry" icon="trash">
    Delete a time entry.

    **Description:**
    Deletes an existing time entry, specified by `timer_id`, from a Workspace identified by `team_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `timer_id` – The time entry ID *(required)*
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Checklist" icon="trash">
    Delete a checklist.

    **Description:**
    Permanently deletes an existing checklist identified by its `checklist_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `checklist_id` – The checklist ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Checklist Item" icon="trash">
    Delete a checklist item.

    **Description:**
    Permanently deletes an existing item, identified by `checklist_item_id`, from an existing checklist, identified by `checklist_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `checklist_id` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `checklist_item_id` – The checklist item ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Comment" icon="trash">
    Delete a comment from a task.

    **Description:**
    Deletes an existing comment from a task using its `comment_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `comment_id` – The comment ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Goal" icon="trash">
    Delete a goal.

    **Description:**
    Permanently removes an existing Goal, identified by its `goal_id`, from the Workspace.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `goal_id` – The goal ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Task" icon="trash">
    Delete a task.

    **Description:**
    Permanently deletes a task, using its standard ID or a custom task ID (requires `custom_task_ids=true` and `team_id`).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `team_id` – Team ID (required if custom_task_ids is true) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Edit Checklist" icon="pen">
    Update a checklist.

    **Description:**
    Updates an existing checklist's name or position, identified by its `checklist_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `checklist_id` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Updated checklist name *(optional)*
    - `position` – Updated position *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Edit Checklist Item" icon="pen">
    Update a checklist item.

    **Description:**
    Updates an existing checklist item, allowing modification of its name, assignee, resolution status, or parent item for nesting.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `checklist_id` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `checklist_item_id` – The checklist item ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Updated item name *(optional)*
    - `assignee` – Updated assignee user ID *(optional)*
    - `resolved` – Resolution status *(optional)*
    - `parent` – Parent item ID for nesting *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Accessible Custom Fields" icon="list">
    Retrieve custom field definitions for a list.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all accessible Custom Field definitions for a specified ClickUp List using its `list_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `list_id` – The list ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Filtered Team Tasks" icon="list">
    Retrieve filtered tasks from a team.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a paginated list of tasks (up to 100 per page) from a specified team (Workspace ID in `team_Id`) based on various filter criteria, respecting user access permissions.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - Filter criteria (status, assignee, due date, etc.) *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Folder" icon="folder">
    Retrieve folder details.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information about a specific folder in ClickUp.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `folder_id` – The folder ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Folderless Lists" icon="list">
    Retrieve lists not in folders.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all Lists within a specified Space that are not located in any Folder.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `space_id` – The space ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Folders" icon="folders">
    Retrieve folders in a space.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves Folders within a specified ClickUp Space, ensuring `space_id` is valid, with an option to filter by archived status.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `space_id` – The space ID *(required)*
    - `archived` – Filter by archived status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Goal" icon="target">
    Retrieve goal details.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information for an existing ClickUp Goal, specified by its unique `goal_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `goal_id` – The goal ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Goals" icon="target">
    Retrieve goals for a workspace.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves goals for a specified ClickUp Workspace (Team); the `team_id` must be valid and accessible.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `include_completed` – Include completed goals *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List" icon="list">
    Retrieve list details.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information for an existing List in ClickUp, identified by its unique `list_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `list_id` – The list ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Comments" icon="comment">
    Retrieve comments for a list.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves comments for a specific ClickUp List, supporting pagination using `start` (timestamp) and `start_id` (comment ID) to fetch earlier comments; omits them for the latest 25.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `list_id` – The list ID *(required)*
    - `start` – Start timestamp for pagination *(optional)*
    - `start_id` – Start comment ID for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get List Members" icon="users">
    Retrieve list members.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all members of a specific, existing ClickUp List by its ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `list_id` – The list ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Lists" icon="list">
    Retrieve lists in a folder.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all lists within a specified, existing ClickUp folder, optionally filtering by archived status.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `folder_id` – The folder ID *(required)*
    - `archived` – Filter by archived status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Running Time Entry" icon="clock">
    Retrieve the active time entry.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves the currently active time entry for a user in a Workspace; a negative 'duration' in its data indicates it's running, and the response may be empty if no entry is active.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `user_id` – The user ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Singular Time Entry" icon="clock">
    Retrieve a specific time entry.

    **Description:**
    Fetches a specific time entry by its ID for a given team; a negative duration in the response indicates an active timer.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `timer_id` – The time entry ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Space" icon="folder">
    Retrieve space details.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information for an existing Space in a ClickUp Workspace, identified by its unique space_id.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `space_id` – The space ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Spaces" icon="folders">
    Retrieve spaces for a team.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves Spaces for a Team ID; member information for private Spaces is returned only if the authenticated user is a member.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `archived` – Filter by archived status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Space Tags" icon="tags">
    Retrieve tags for a space.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all tags for tasks within a specified ClickUp Space, requiring a valid `space_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `space_id` – The space ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Task" icon="file">
    Retrieve task details.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves comprehensive details for a ClickUp task by its ID, supporting standard or custom task IDs (requires `team_id` for custom IDs).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `team_id` – Team ID (required for custom task IDs) *(optional)*
    - `include_subtasks` – Include subtasks *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Task Comments" icon="comment">
    Retrieve comments for a task.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves up to 25 comments for a specified task, supporting pagination using `start` and `start_id` to fetch older comments.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `start` – Start timestamp for pagination *(optional)*
    - `start_id` – Start comment ID for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Task Members" icon="users">
    Retrieve task members.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves users with explicit access (directly assigned or shared) to a specific existing task, excluding users with inherited permissions.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Tasks" icon="list">
    Retrieve tasks from a list.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves tasks from a specified ClickUp list; only tasks whose home is the given list_id are returned.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `list_id` – The list ID *(required)*
    - `archived` – Filter by archived status *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Task S Time In Status" icon="clock">
    Retrieve time spent in each status.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves the duration a task has spent in each status, provided the "Total time in Status" ClickApp is enabled for the Workspace.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Task Templates" icon="file">
    Retrieve task templates.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves task templates for a specified Workspace (Team ID), supporting pagination.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `page` – Page number for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Time Entries Within A Date Range" icon="clock">
    Retrieve time entries in a date range.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves time entries for a specified Team (Workspace ID) within a date range (defaults to the last 30 days for the authenticated user if dates are omitted); active timers are indicated by negative durations in the response.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `start_date` – Start date timestamp *(optional)*
    - `end_date` – End date timestamp *(optional)*
    - `assignee` – Filter by assignee user ID *(optional)*
    - `include_task_tags` – Include task tags *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Time Entry History" icon="clock">
    Retrieve time entry modification history.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves the modification history for an existing time entry within a specific ClickUp Team (Workspace).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `timer_id` – The time entry ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get View Tasks" icon="list">
    Retrieve tasks from a view.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all tasks visible in a specified ClickUp view, respecting its applied filters, sorting, and grouping.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `view_id` – The view ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Remove Custom Field Value" icon="trash">
    Remove a custom field value from a task.

    **Description:**
    Removes an existing value from a Custom Field on a specific task; this does not delete the Custom Field definition or its predefined options.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `field_id` – The custom field ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Remove Guest From Task" icon="user-minus">
    Remove a guest from a task.

    **Description:**
    Revokes a guest's access to a specific task; only available for Workspaces on the ClickUp Enterprise Plan.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `guest_id` – The guest user ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Remove Tag From Task" icon="tag">
    Remove a tag from a task.

    **Description:**
    Removes a tag from a specified task by disassociating it (does not delete the tag from Workspace), succeeding even if the tag is not on the task.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `tag_name` – The tag name to remove *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Remove Task From List" icon="list">
    Remove a task from an additional list.

    **Description:**
    Removes a task from an extra list (not its home list); the "Tasks in Multiple Lists" ClickApp must be enabled.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `list_id` – The list ID to remove from *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Set Custom Field Value" icon="pen">
    Set or update a custom field value.

    **Description:**
    Sets or updates a Custom Field's value for a task; the new value (with type-dependent structure, e.g., `{"value": "text"}` or `{"value": 123, "value_options": {"currency_type": "USD"}}`) is provided in the JSON request body.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `field_id` – The custom field ID *(required)*
    - `value` – The field value (structure depends on field type) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Start A Time Entry" icon="play">
    Start a new time entry timer.

    **Description:**
    Starts a new time entry (timer) in the specified Team (Workspace), optionally associating it with a task, adding a description, setting billable status, or applying tags (tags feature requires Business Plan or higher).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(optional)*
    - `description` – Time entry description *(optional)*
    - `billable` – Whether the entry is billable *(optional)*
    - `tags` – Array of tag names *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Stop A Time Entry" icon="stop">
    Stop the active time entry.

    **Description:**
    Stops the authenticated user's currently active time entry in the specified Team (Workspace), which requires an existing time entry to be running.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update A Time Entry" icon="pen">
    Update an existing time entry.

    **Description:**
    Updates an existing ClickUp time entry; provide `start` and `end` times together, and include `team_id` as a query param (request field `team_id_1`) if `custom_task_ids` is true.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `timer_id` – The time entry ID *(required)*
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `start` – Updated start time *(optional)*
    - `end` – Updated end time *(optional)*
    - `duration` – Updated duration *(optional)*
    - `description` – Updated description *(optional)*
    - `billable` – Updated billable status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Comment" icon="pen">
    Update a task comment.

    **Description:**
    Updates an existing task comment's text, assignee (who must be a valid workspace member), or resolution status, requiring a valid existing comment_id.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `comment_id` – The comment ID *(required)*
    - `comment_text` – Updated comment text *(optional)*
    - `assignee` – Updated assignee user ID *(optional)*
    - `resolved` – Resolution status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Goal" icon="pen">
    Update a goal.

    **Description:**
    Updates attributes of an existing ClickUp goal, identified by its `goal_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `goal_id` – The goal ID *(required)*
    - Updated goal attributes (name, due_date, etc.) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update List" icon="pen">
    Update list attributes.

    **Description:**
    Updates attributes of an existing ClickUp list, such as its name, content, due date, priority, assignee, or color status, identified by its `list_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `list_id` – The list ID *(required)*
    - Updated list attributes (name, due_date, priority, etc.) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Task" icon="pen">
    Update task attributes.

    **Description:**
    Updates attributes of an existing task; `team_id` is required if `custom_task_ids` is true, use a single space (" ") for `description` to clear it, and provide at least one modifiable field.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `team_id` – Team ID (required if custom_task_ids is true) *(optional)*
    - Updated task attributes (name, description, status, assignees, due_date, etc.) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-close.com"
    alt="Close"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Close</h2>
</div>

Close is a CRM platform designed to help businesses manage and streamline their sales processes, including calling, email automation, and predictive dialers.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Create Call" icon="phone">
    Creates a new call record in Close.com. This tool allows you to log both inbound and outbound calls associated with a lead.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `lead_id` – The ID of the lead associated with the call *(required)*
    - `direction` – Call direction: "inbound" or "outbound" *(required)*
    - `contact_id` – The ID of the contact *(optional)*
    - `phone` – Phone number used for the call *(optional)*
    - `duration` – Call duration in seconds *(optional)*
    - `note` – Notes or summary of the call *(optional)*
    - `recording_url` – URL to the call recording *(optional)*
    - `user_id` – The ID of the user who made/received the call *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Lead" icon="user-plus">
    Creates a new lead in Close CRM with basic company information and optional contact details.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `company_name` – Name of the company *(required)*
    - `description` – Description or notes about the lead *(optional)*
    - `website` – Company website URL *(optional)*
    - `status` – Lead status (e.g., "potential", "qualified", "customer") *(optional)*
    - `contacts` – Array of contact information *(optional)*
    - `addresses` – Array of address information *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create SMS" icon="message">
    Creates a new SMS message in Close. The tool allows sending immediate SMS messages or logging received SMS messages.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `local_phone` – Your phone number (the number sending/receiving) *(required)*
    - `remote_phone` – The other party's phone number *(required)*
    - `text` – The SMS message content *(required)*
    - `status` – Message status (e.g., "sent", "received") *(optional)*
    - `source` – Source of the SMS *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Task" icon="list-check">
    Creates a new task in Close.com. Tasks are used to track to-do items and can be associated with leads.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `text` – Task description or title *(required)*
    - `due_date` – Due date for the task in ISO 8601 format *(optional)*
    - `is_complete` – Whether the task is already completed *(optional)*
    - `lead_id` – The ID of the lead to associate with the task *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Call" icon="trash">
    Deletes a specific call activity in Close.com. Useful for removing incorrectly logged calls or cleaning up call records.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `call_id` – The unique ID of the call to delete *(required)*

    <Warning>
      **Cannot be undone:** This action permanently deletes the call record and cannot be reversed.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Note" icon="note-sticky">
    Retrieves a list of note activities from Close. Allows users to fetch notes with optional filtering parameters.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `lead_id` – Filter notes by lead ID *(optional)*
    - `user_id` – Filter notes by user ID *(optional)*
    - `date_from` – Start date for filtering notes *(optional)*
    - `date_to` – End date for filtering notes *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/Screenshot_2025-10-24_at_3.51.32PM.png"
    alt="Composio Search"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Composio Search</h2>
</div>

Composio Search provides comprehensive web search across travel (flights, hotels, events), e-commerce (Amazon, Walmart, shopping), financial markets, news, academic research, images, and location services.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Amazon" icon="amazon">
    Search Amazon for products across different country marketplaces. This tool searches Amazon's product catalog with support for multiple international Amazon domains/marketplaces.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Product search query *(required)*
    - `domain` – Amazon marketplace domain (e.g., "amazon.com", "amazon.co.uk") *(optional)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of results to return *(optional)*

    <Tip>
      Each Amazon domain serves different countries with local pricing, currency, shipping options, and product availability.
    </Tip>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Duck Duck Go" icon="search">
    Perform web searches using DuckDuckGo search engine. Focuses on web information and details without tracking.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query *(required)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of results to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Event" icon="calendar-days">
    Search for upcoming events, concerts, festivals, conferences, and other activities. Finds local and global events with powerful filtering options.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Event search query *(required)*
    - `location` – City, neighborhood, or address for location-based search *(optional)*
    - `date` – Date filter (e.g., "today", "tomorrow", "weekend", "next week") *(optional)*
    - `virtual` – Filter for virtual events *(optional)*
    - `language` – Language for results (100+ languages supported) *(optional)*
    - `country` – Country code for international search *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Finance" icon="chart-line">
    Get real-time stock prices, market data, financial news, and company information with historical analysis.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Stock symbol, company name, or financial query *(required)*
    - `time_range` – Time range for historical data (1D, 1W, 1M, 3M, 6M, 1Y, MAX) *(optional)*
    - `include_news` – Include financial news in results *(optional)*

    <Tip>
      Returns detailed graph data, summary information, and key events for 6M+ time windows.
    </Tip>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Flights" icon="plane">
    Search for flights with comprehensive pricing, schedule, and airline information. Finds available flights between cities/airports with detailed pricing.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `origin` – Departure city or airport code *(required)*
    - `destination` – Arrival city or airport code *(required)*
    - `departure_date` – Departure date in ISO 8601 format *(required)*
    - `return_date` – Return date for round-trip flights *(optional)*
    - `adults` – Number of adult passengers *(optional)*
    - `children` – Number of child passengers *(optional)*
    - `infants` – Number of infant passengers *(optional)*
    - `class` – Travel class (economy, business, first) *(optional)*
    - `currency` – Currency for pricing *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Google Maps" icon="map">
    Perform location-specific searches using Google Maps. Fetches the most relevant location data based on the input query.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Location search query *(required)*
    - `location` – Specific location or area to search within *(optional)*
    - `type` – Type of place (e.g., "restaurant", "hotel", "gas_station") *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Hotels" icon="hotel">
    Search for hotels and vacation rentals with comprehensive filtering and pricing. Finds available accommodations with detailed information.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `location` – Destination city or address *(required)*
    - `check_in` – Check-in date in ISO 8601 format *(required)*
    - `check_out` – Check-out date in ISO 8601 format *(required)*
    - `adults` – Number of adult guests *(optional)*
    - `children` – Number of child guests *(optional)*
    - `price_min` – Minimum price per night *(optional)*
    - `price_max` – Maximum price per night *(optional)*
    - `stars` – Minimum star rating *(optional)*
    - `sort_by` – Sort by price, rating, or distance *(optional)*
    - `free_cancellation` – Filter for free cancellation options *(optional)*
    - `include_vacation_rentals` – Include vacation rentals in results *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Shopping" icon="shopping-cart">
    Search for products with advanced price filtering, location targeting, and deal discovery. Provides comprehensive product search across multiple retailers.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Product search query *(required)*
    - `price_min` – Minimum price filter *(optional)*
    - `price_max` – Maximum price filter *(optional)*
    - `location` – Geographic location for local retailers *(optional)*
    - `sort_by` – Sort by price (low to high, high to low) *(optional)*
    - `free_shipping` – Filter for free shipping options *(optional)*
    - `on_sale` – Filter for sale items only *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Tavily" icon="brain">
    Perform advanced searches using Tavily LLM Search API. Accommodates complex queries with multiple filtering options for fine-tuned results.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query (supports keyword and phrase searches) *(required)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `include_domains` – Specific domains to include in search *(optional)*
    - `exclude_domains` – Domains to exclude from search *(optional)*
    - `search_depth` – Depth of search (basic or advanced) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Trip Advisor" icon="map-location-dot">
    Search TripAdvisor for travel recommendations and itinerary planning. Searches TripAdvisor's comprehensive travel database for attractions, restaurants, hotels, tours, and activities.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query for attractions, restaurants, hotels, or activities *(required)*
    - `location` – Destination city or location *(optional)*
    - `type` – Type of result (attraction, restaurant, hotel, tour) *(optional)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of results to return *(optional)*

    <Tip>
      Returns detailed information including ratings, reviews, photos, and traveler recommendations.
    </Tip>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Walmart" icon="store">
    Search Walmart for products with price filtering. Searches Walmart's product catalog including groceries, electronics, clothing, home goods, pharmacy, and auto services.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Product search query *(required)*
    - `price_min` – Minimum price filter *(optional)*
    - `price_max` – Maximum price filter *(optional)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of results to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Web" icon="globe">
    Perform general web searches and find relevant information. Searches the web for information on any topic.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query *(required)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of results to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/discordbot.svg"
    alt="Discord Bot"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Discord Bot</h2>
</div>

Discordbot refers to automated programs on Discord servers, performing tasks like moderation, music playback, and user engagement to enhance community interactions.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Add Group DM User" icon="user-plus">
    Adds a user to a Discord group Direct Message (DM) channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the group DM channel *(required)*
    - `user_id` – The ID of the user to add *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add My Message Reaction" icon="thumbs-up">
    Adds an emoji reaction from the authenticated user/bot to a specific message in a Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel containing the message *(required)*
    - `message_id` – The ID of the message to react to *(required)*
    - `emoji` – The emoji to add (unicode or custom emoji ID) *(required)*

    <Note>
      This action does not return information about existing reactions on the message.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Channel Invite" icon="link">
    Creates a new invite for the specified Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel to create an invite for *(required)*
    - `max_age` – Invite expiration time in seconds (0 for never) *(optional)*
    - `max_uses` – Maximum number of uses (0 for unlimited) *(optional)*
    - `temporary` – Whether the invite grants temporary membership *(optional)*
    - `unique` – Whether to reuse a similar invite if available *(optional)*

    <Warning>
      Requires 'CREATE_INSTANT_INVITE' permission for the channel.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create DM" icon="envelope">
    Creates a new direct message (DM) channel or retrieves an existing one.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `recipient_id` – User ID for a 1-on-1 DM *(optional)*
    - `access_tokens` – Access tokens for a group DM *(optional)*

    <Note>
      This action only establishes or fetches the channel and does not send messages.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Guild Scheduled Event" icon="calendar-days">
    Creates a new scheduled event in a Discord guild.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `guild_id` – The ID of the guild *(required)*
    - `name` – Event name *(required)*
    - `description` – Event description *(optional)*
    - `scheduled_start_time` – Start time in ISO 8601 format *(required)*
    - `scheduled_end_time` – End time in ISO 8601 format *(optional)*
    - `entity_type` – Event type (e.g., STAGE_INSTANCE, VOICE, EXTERNAL) *(required)*
    - `privacy_level` – Privacy level (GUILD_ONLY) *(optional)*

    <Tip>
      Event details depend on the `entity_type` - different types require different fields in the request body.
    </Tip>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Message" icon="message">
    Sends a message to a specified Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel to send the message to *(required)*
    - `content` – Message text content *(optional)*
    - `embeds` – Array of embed objects *(optional)*
    - `sticker_ids` – Array of sticker IDs *(optional)*
    - `components` – Array of message components *(optional)*
    - `attachments` – Array of attachment objects *(optional)*

    <Warning>
      Requires `SEND_MESSAGES` permission and at least one of: `content`, `embeds`, `sticker_ids`, or `attachments`.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Guild Scheduled Event" icon="trash">
    Permanently deletes a specific scheduled event from a Discord guild.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `guild_id` – The ID of the guild *(required)*
    - `event_id` – The ID of the event to delete *(required)*

    <Warning>
      **Irreversible:** This action permanently deletes the event and cannot be undone.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Message" icon="trash">
    Permanently deletes a message from a specified Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel containing the message *(required)*
    - `message_id` – The ID of the message to delete *(required)*

    <Warning>
      **Irreversible:** This action permanently deletes the message and cannot be undone.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete User Message Reaction" icon="thumbs-down">
    Removes a specific user's emoji reaction from a message.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel containing the message *(required)*
    - `message_id` – The ID of the message *(required)*
    - `emoji` – The emoji to remove (unicode or custom emoji ID) *(required)*
    - `user_id` – The ID of the user whose reaction to remove *(optional)*

    <Warning>
      Requires 'Manage Messages' permission if deleting reactions from other users.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Channel" icon="hashtag">
    Retrieves detailed metadata for a specific Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel to retrieve *(required)*

    <Note>
      Returns only channel metadata, not message content or member lists.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Guild Member" icon="users">
    Retrieves detailed information for a specific member of a Discord guild.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `guild_id` – The ID of the guild *(required)*
    - `user_id` – The ID of the member to retrieve *(required)*

    <Note>
      Requires the bot to belong to the guild and have necessary permissions (e.g., GUILD_MEMBERS intent).
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Guild Scheduled Event" icon="calendar-check">
    Retrieves a specific scheduled event from a Discord guild by its ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `guild_id` – The ID of the guild *(required)*
    - `event_id` – The ID of the event to retrieve *(required)*
    - `with_user_count` – Whether to include subscribed user count *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Message" icon="message">
    Retrieves a specific message from a Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel containing the message *(required)*
    - `message_id` – The ID of the message to retrieve *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Thread Member" icon="comments">
    Retrieves a member from a specified thread using their user ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the thread *(required)*
    - `user_id` – The ID of the thread member to retrieve *(required)*
    - `with_member` – Whether to include the full guild member object *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get User" icon="user">
    Fetches public information for a Discord user.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user_id` – The ID of the user to retrieve *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Invite Resolve" icon="link">
    Resolves a Discord invite code to get its details.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `invite_code` – The invite code to resolve *(required)*
    - `with_counts` – Whether to include member counts *(optional)*
    - `with_expiration` – Whether to include expiration time *(optional)*
    - `guild_scheduled_event_id` – Specific guild scheduled event ID *(optional)*

    <Note>
      Visibility of some details may depend on bot permissions.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Join Thread" icon="comments">
    Joins the authenticated user to a thread specified by channel_id.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the thread to join *(required)*

    <Note>
      Use this when the user is not already a member, for archived threads, or for threads requiring explicit joining. The thread must be joinable, not locked or full, and the user must have permissions.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Channel Invites" icon="list">
    Fetches all active invites for a given Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel to list invites for *(required)*

    <Note>
      Requires channel invite view permissions. Response object structures may vary.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Channel Webhooks" icon="webhook">
    Fetches detailed information for all webhooks in a given Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel to list webhooks for *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Guild Members" icon="users">
    Retrieves members for a Discord guild.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `guild_id` – The ID of the guild *(required)*
    - `limit` – Maximum number of members to return *(optional)*
    - `after` – User ID to return members after *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Guild Scheduled Events" icon="calendar">
    Retrieves a list of scheduled events for a specified Discord guild.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `guild_id` – The ID of the guild *(required)*
    - `with_user_count` – Whether to include subscribed user counts *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Guild Scheduled Event Users" icon="user-group">
    Fetches users who have expressed interest in a specific scheduled event.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `guild_id` – The ID of the guild *(required)*
    - `event_id` – The ID of the scheduled event *(required)*
    - `limit` – Maximum number of users to return *(optional)*
    - `with_member` – Whether to include full guild member objects *(optional)*
    - `before` – User ID to return users before *(optional)*
    - `after` – User ID to return users after *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Messages" icon="message-lines">
    Retrieves historical messages from a specified Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel to retrieve messages from *(required)*
    - `limit` – Maximum number of messages to return (1-100) *(optional)*
    - `around` – Message ID to get messages around *(optional)*
    - `before` – Message ID to get messages before *(optional)*
    - `after` – Message ID to get messages after *(optional)*

    <Note>
      Messages are typically returned newest first. For real-time messages, use Discord's WebSocket Gateway API.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Pinned Messages" icon="thumbtack">
    Retrieves all currently pinned messages from a Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel to retrieve pinned messages from *(required)*

    <Note>
      Typically limited to 50 messages, and no history of past pins is returned.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Search Guild Members" icon="search">
    Searches for members in a specific Discord guild, allowing filtering by a query string.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `guild_id` – The ID of the guild to search in *(required)*
    - `query` – Search query string *(required)*
    - `limit` – Maximum number of results to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Unpin Message" icon="thumbtack">
    Unpins a message that is currently pinned in a specified Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel containing the pinned message *(required)*
    - `message_id` – The ID of the message to unpin *(required)*

    <Note>
      The message itself is not deleted, only unpinned.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Application Command" icon="gear">
    Updates specified properties of a Discord application command.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `application_id` – The ID of the application *(required)*
    - `command_id` – The ID of the command to update *(required)*
    - `name` – New command name *(optional)*
    - `description` – New command description *(optional)*
    - `options` – Array of command options *(optional)*

    <Warning>
      Omitted properties remain unchanged. The `options` field, if provided, overwrites all existing options.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Guild Scheduled Event" icon="calendar-pen">
    Updates attributes for an existing Discord guild event.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `guild_id` – The ID of the guild *(required)*
    - `event_id` – The ID of the event to update *(required)*
    - `name` – New event name *(optional)*
    - `description` – New event description *(optional)*
    - `scheduled_start_time` – New start time *(optional)*
    - `scheduled_end_time` – New end time *(optional)*
    - `status` – New event status *(optional)*
    - `location` – New event location *(optional)*

    <Note>
      Only fields in the request body are changed.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Message" icon="pen">
    Updates a message previously sent by the bot in a Discord channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel_id` – The ID of the channel containing the message *(required)*
    - `message_id` – The ID of the message to update *(required)*
    - `content` – New message content *(optional)*
    - `embeds` – New embed array *(optional)*
    - `components` – New components array *(optional)*
    - `flags` – Message flags *(optional)*

    <Warning>
      Only provide fields to change. Use null or an empty list to clear existing values. New attachments cannot be uploaded.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

**Available Tools:**

  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-freshdesk.com"
    alt="Freshdesk"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Freshdesk</h2>
</div>

Freshdesk provides customer support software with ticketing, knowledge base, and automation features for efficient helpdesk operations and better customer experiences.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Create Ticket" icon="ticket">
    Creates a new ticket in Freshdesk.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `subject` – Ticket subject or title *(required)*
    - `description` – Ticket description or details *(required)*
    - `email` – Requester's email address *(optional)*
    - `priority` – Ticket priority level (1-4) *(optional)*
    - `status` – Ticket status (e.g., "open", "pending", "resolved") *(optional)*
    - `type` – Ticket type (e.g., "question", "incident", "problem") *(optional)*
    - `tags` – Array of tags for the ticket *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="View Ticket" icon="eye">
    Views an existing ticket in Freshdesk.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `ticket_id` – The ID of the ticket to view *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Tickets" icon="list">
    Retrieves a list of tickets from Freshdesk.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `filter` – Filter criteria (e.g., status, priority, requester) *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Maximum number of tickets to return *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List All Tickets" icon="list-check">
    Lists all tickets in Freshdesk.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Maximum number of tickets to return *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Ticket" icon="pen">
    Updates an existing ticket in Freshdesk.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `ticket_id` – The ID of the ticket to update *(required)*
    - `subject` – Updated ticket subject *(optional)*
    - `description` – Updated ticket description *(optional)*
    - `priority` – Updated priority level *(optional)*
    - `status` – Updated ticket status *(optional)*
    - `tags` – Updated tags array *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Reply Ticket" icon="reply">
    Replies to an existing ticket in Freshdesk.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `ticket_id` – The ID of the ticket to reply to *(required)*
    - `body` – Reply message content *(required)*
    - `cc_emails` – Array of CC email addresses *(optional)*
    - `private` – Whether the reply is private/internal *(optional)*
    - `attachments` – Array of attachment file IDs *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Ticket" icon="trash">
    Deletes an existing ticket in Freshdesk.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `ticket_id` – The ID of the ticket to delete *(required)*

    <Warning>
      **Irreversible:** This action permanently deletes the ticket and cannot be undone.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-gmail_lvO35bh.com"
    alt="Gmail"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Gmail</h2>
</div>

Gmail is Google's email service, featuring spam protection, search functions, and seamless integration with other G Suite apps for productivity.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Send Email" icon="envelope">
    Sends an email via Gmail API using the authenticated user's Google profile display name.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `recipient_email` – Recipient email address(es) *(required if cc/bcc not provided)*
    - `cc` – CC email address(es) *(optional)*
    - `bcc` – BCC email address(es) *(optional)*
    - `subject` – Email subject line *(required if body not provided)*
    - `body` – Email body content *(required if subject not provided)*
    - `is_html` – Whether the body contains HTML content *(optional)*
    - `attachments` – Array of attachment objects with s3key, mimetype, and name *(optional)*

    <Warning>
      At least one of recipient_email, cc, or bcc must be provided. At least one of subject or body must be provided. Set `is_html=True` if the body contains HTML.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Email Draft" icon="file-pen">
    Creates a Gmail email draft without sending it.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `recipient_email` – Recipient email address(es) *(required if cc/bcc not provided)*
    - `cc` – CC email address(es) *(optional)*
    - `bcc` – BCC email address(es) *(optional)*
    - `subject` – Email subject line *(required if body not provided)*
    - `body` – Email body content *(required if subject not provided)*
    - `is_html` – Whether the body contains HTML content *(optional)*
    - `attachments` – Array of attachment objects *(optional)*
    - `thread_id` – Thread ID for threading replies *(optional)*

    <Warning>
      At least one of recipient_email, cc, or bcc must be provided. At least one of subject or body must be provided. Set `is_html=True` for HTML content.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Send Draft" icon="paper-plane">
    Sends an existing draft email to its recipients.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `draft_id` – The ID of the draft to send *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Emails" icon="inbox">
    Fetches a list of email messages from a Gmail account, supporting filtering, pagination, and optional full content retrieval.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Gmail search query (e.g., "from:example@gmail.com") *(optional)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of emails to return *(optional)*
    - `page_token` – Token for pagination *(optional)*
    - `include_body` – Whether to include full email body content *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Message By Message Id" icon="envelope-open">
    Fetches a specific email message by its ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `message_id` – The ID of the message to retrieve *(required)*
    - `format` – Format to return (full, metadata, minimal) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Message By Thread Id" icon="comments">
    Retrieves messages from a Gmail thread using its thread ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `thread_id` – The ID of the thread to retrieve *(required)*
    - `format` – Format to return (full, metadata, minimal) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Reply To Thread" icon="reply">
    Sends a reply within a specific Gmail thread using the original thread's subject.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `thread_id` – The ID of the thread to reply to *(required)*
    - `recipient_email` – Recipient email address(es) *(required if cc/bcc not provided)*
    - `cc` – CC email address(es) *(optional)*
    - `bcc` – BCC email address(es) *(optional)*
    - `body` – Reply message content *(required)*
    - `attachments` – Array of attachment objects with s3key, mimetype, and name *(optional)*

    <Warning>
      At least one of recipient_email, cc, or bcc must be provided.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Forward Message" icon="share">
    Forwards an existing Gmail message to specified recipients, preserving original body and attachments.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `message_id` – The ID of the message to forward *(required)*
    - `recipient_email` – Forward recipient email address(es) *(required)*
    - `cc` – CC email address(es) *(optional)*
    - `bcc` – BCC email address(es) *(optional)*
    - `body` – Additional message to include with forward *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Threads" icon="list">
    Retrieves a list of email threads from a Gmail account, supporting filtering and pagination.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Gmail search query for filtering threads *(optional)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of threads to return *(optional)*
    - `page_token` – Token for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Drafts" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieves a paginated list of email drafts from a user's Gmail account.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of drafts to return *(optional)*
    - `page_token` – Token for pagination *(optional)*
    - `verbose` – Whether to get full draft details including subject, body, sender, and timestamp *(optional)*

    <Tip>
      Use `verbose=true` to get full draft details including subject, body, sender, and timestamp.
    </Tip>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Labels" icon="tags">
    Retrieves a list of all system and user-created labels for the specified Gmail account.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None required*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Label To Email" icon="tag">
    Adds and/or removes specified Gmail labels for a message.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `message_id` – The ID of the message to label *(required)*
    - `add_label_ids` – Array of label IDs to add *(optional)*
    - `remove_label_ids` – Array of label IDs to remove *(optional)*

    <Note>
      Ensure `message_id` and all `label_ids` are valid. Use 'List Labels' for custom label IDs.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Modify Thread Labels" icon="tags">
    Adds or removes specified existing label IDs from a Gmail thread, affecting all its messages.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `thread_id` – The ID of the thread to modify *(required)*
    - `add_label_ids` – Array of label IDs to add *(optional)*
    - `remove_label_ids` – Array of label IDs to remove *(optional)*

    <Note>
      Ensure the thread ID is valid. This affects all messages in the thread.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Contacts" icon="address-book">
    Fetches contacts (connections) for the authenticated Google account, allowing selection of specific data fields and pagination.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `page_size` – Number of contacts to return per page *(optional)*
    - `page_token` – Token for pagination *(optional)*
    - `person_fields` – Comma-separated list of fields to return (e.g., "names,emailAddresses") *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get People" icon="user">
    Retrieves either a specific person's details or lists 'Other Contacts', with person_fields specifying the data to return.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `resource_name` – Resource name of the person to retrieve (e.g., "people/123456789") *(optional)*
    - `other_contacts` – Whether to list 'Other Contacts' instead *(optional)*
    - `person_fields` – Comma-separated list of fields to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Search People" icon="search">
    Searches contacts by matching the query against names, nicknames, emails, phone numbers, and organizations.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query string *(required)*
    - `read_mask` – Comma-separated list of fields to return *(optional)*
    - `include_other_contacts` – Whether to include 'Other Contacts' in search *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/googlecalendar_gX71Vlt.svg"
    alt="Google Calendar"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Google Calendar</h2>
</div>

Google Calendar is a time management tool providing scheduling features, event reminders, and integration with email and other apps for streamlined organization.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Create Event" icon="calendar-plus">
    Create a Google Calendar event using start_datetime plus duration fields to derive the end time.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The ID of the calendar (use "primary" for main calendar) *(required)*
    - `start_datetime` – Start date and time in ISO 8601 format (e.g., "2025-01-16T13:00:00") *(required)*
    - `timezone` – Timezone in IANA format (e.g., "America/New_York") *(required)*
    - `event_duration_hour` – Duration hours *(optional)*
    - `event_duration_minutes` – Duration minutes *(optional)*
    - `summary` – Event title or summary *(required)*
    - `description` – Event description *(optional)*
    - `location` – Event location *(optional)*
    - `attendees` – Array of attendee objects with email addresses *(optional)*
    - `exclude_organizer` – Whether to exclude organizer from attendees *(optional)*

    <Tip>
      Example: Create a 1 hour 30 minute event: `{"calendar_id": "primary", "start_datetime": "2025-01-16T13:00:00", "timezone": "America/New_York", "event_duration_hour": 1, "event_duration_minutes": 30, "summary": "Client sync", "attendees": [{"email": "guest@example.com"}]}`
    </Tip>

    <Warning>
      Requires calendar write access. The organizer is added as an attendee unless `exclude_organizer` is True.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Quick Add" icon="bolt">
    Parses natural language text to quickly create a basic Google Calendar event with its title, date, and time.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The ID of the calendar (use "primary" for main calendar) *(optional)*
    - `text` – Natural language text describing the event (e.g., "Meeting tomorrow at 2pm") *(required)*

    <Note>
      Suitable for simple scheduling only. Does not support direct attendee addition or recurring events. Calendar ID must be valid if not 'primary'.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Event" icon="pen">
    Updates an existing event by event_id in a Google Calendar using full PUT replacement.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The ID of the calendar containing the event *(required)*
    - `event_id` – The ID of the event to update *(required)*
    - `start_datetime` – Updated start date and time *(optional)*
    - `end_datetime` – Updated end date and time *(optional)*
    - `summary` – Updated event title *(optional)*
    - `description` – Updated event description *(optional)*
    - `location` – Updated event location *(optional)*
    - `attendees` – Updated array of attendees *(optional)*

    <Warning>
      This is a full PUT replacement—provide all desired fields as unspecified ones may be cleared or reset.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Patch Event" icon="pen">
    Update specified fields of an existing event in a Google Calendar using patch semantics.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The ID of the calendar containing the event *(required)*
    - `event_id` – The ID of the event to patch *(required)*
    - `summary` – Updated event title *(optional)*
    - `description` – Updated event description *(optional)*
    - `location` – Updated event location *(optional)*
    - `start_datetime` – Updated start date and time *(optional)*
    - `end_datetime` – Updated end date and time *(optional)*
    - `attendees` – Updated array of attendees *(optional)*

    <Warning>
      Array fields like `attendees` are fully replaced if provided. Ensure calendar_id and event_id are valid and user has write access.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Event" icon="trash">
    Deletes a specified event by event_id from a Google Calendar.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The ID of the calendar containing the event *(required)*
    - `event_id` – The ID of the event to delete *(required)*

    <Warning>
      **Irreversible:** This action permanently deletes the event. This action is idempotent and raises a 404 error if the event is not found.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Events List" icon="list">
    Returns events on the specified calendar.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The ID of the calendar to list events from *(required)*
    - `time_min` – Lower bound (exclusive) for an event's start time *(optional)*
    - `time_max` – Upper bound (exclusive) for an event's end time *(optional)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of events to return *(optional)*
    - `page_token` – Token for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Find Event" icon="search">
    Finds events in a specified Google Calendar using text query, time ranges, and event types.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The ID of the calendar to search *(required)*
    - `query` – Text query to search for in event titles and descriptions *(optional)*
    - `time_min` – Lower bound for event start time *(optional)*
    - `time_max` – Upper bound for event end time *(optional)*
    - `updated_min` – Lower bound for last modification time *(optional)*
    - `event_types` – Array of event types to filter by *(optional)*

    <Warning>
      Ensure `timeMin` is not chronologically after `timeMax` if both are provided.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Events Instances" icon="repeat">
    Returns instances of the specified recurring event.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The ID of the calendar containing the recurring event *(required)*
    - `event_id` – The ID of the recurring event master *(required)*
    - `time_min` – Lower bound for instance start time *(optional)*
    - `time_max` – Upper bound for instance start time *(optional)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of instances to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Events Move" icon="arrows-rotate">
    Moves an event to another calendar, i.e., changes an event's organizer.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The ID of the source calendar *(required)*
    - `event_id` – The ID of the event to move *(required)*
    - `destination_calendar_id` – The ID of the destination calendar *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Remove Attendee" icon="user-minus">
    Removes an attendee from a specified event in a Google Calendar.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The ID of the calendar containing the event *(required)*
    - `event_id` – The ID of the event *(required)*
    - `attendee_email` – Email address of the attendee to remove *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Find Free Slots" icon="clock">
    Finds both free and busy time slots in Google Calendars for specified calendars within a defined time range.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_ids` – Array of calendar IDs to check *(required)*
    - `time_min` – Start of time range in ISO 8601 format *(optional)*
    - `time_max` – End of time range in ISO 8601 format *(optional)*
    - `timezone` – Timezone for the time range *(optional)*

    <Tip>
      Returns busy intervals enriched with event details and calculates free slots by finding gaps between busy periods. Defaults to the current day UTC if time_min/time_max are omitted.
    </Tip>

    <Warning>
      `time_min` must precede `time_max` if both are provided.
    </Warning>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Free Busy Query" icon="calendar-check">
    Returns free/busy information for a set of calendars.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_ids` – Array of calendar IDs to query *(required)*
    - `time_min` – Start of time range in ISO 8601 format *(required)*
    - `time_max` – End of time range in ISO 8601 format *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Calendars" icon="calendar">
    Retrieves a paginated list of calendars from the user's calendar list.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `min_access_role` – Minimum access role to filter by *(optional)*
    - `page_token` – Token for pagination *(optional)*
    - `sync_token` – Token for incremental sync *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Calendar" icon="calendar-days">
    Retrieves a specific Google Calendar, identified by calendar_id.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – The ID of the calendar to retrieve *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Current Date Time" icon="clock">
    Gets the current date and time, allowing for a specific timezone offset.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `timezone` – Timezone in IANA format (e.g., "America/New_York") *(optional)*

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/google_maps.svg"
    alt="Google Maps"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Google Maps</h2>
</div>

Integrate Google Maps to access location data, geocoding, directions, and mapping services in your application.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Get Route" icon="route">
    Calculates one or more routes between two specified locations using various travel modes and preferences.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `origin` – Starting location address or coordinates *(required)*
    - `destination` – Destination location address or coordinates *(required)*
    - `travel_mode` – Travel mode (e.g., "DRIVE", "WALK", "TRANSIT", "BICYCLE") *(optional)*
    - `avoid` – Route restrictions (e.g., "tolls", "highways", "ferries") *(optional)*
    - `waypoints` – Array of intermediate waypoints *(optional)*
    - `alternatives` – Whether to return alternative routes *(optional)*

    <Note>
      Addresses must be resolvable by Google Maps.
    </Note>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Compute Route Matrix" icon="map-location-dot">
    Calculates travel distance and duration matrix between multiple origins and destinations using the modern Routes API.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `origins` – Array of origin locations (addresses or coordinates) *(required)*
    - `destinations` – Array of destination locations (addresses or coordinates) *(required)*
    - `travel_mode` – Travel mode (e.g., "DRIVE", "WALK", "TRANSIT") *(optional)*
    - `routing_preference` – Routing preference (e.g., "TRAFFIC_AWARE", "TRAFFIC_AWARE_OPTIMAL") *(optional)*

    <Tip>
      Supports OAuth2 authentication and various travel modes. Useful for comparing multiple origin-destination pairs.
    </Tip>

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Text Search" icon="search">
    Searches for places on Google Maps using a textual query.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query text (e.g., "restaurants in London", "Eiffel Tower") *(required)*
    - `location` – Location bias (latitude, longitude) *(optional)*
    - `radius` – Search radius in meters *(optional)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of results to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Nearby Search" icon="map-pin">
    Searches for places (e.g., restaurants, parks) within a specified circular area.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `location` – Center point (latitude, longitude) *(required)*
    - `radius` – Search radius in meters *(required)*
    - `type` – Place type filter (e.g., "restaurant", "park", "gas_station") *(optional)*
    - `keyword` – Keyword search term *(optional)*
    - `max_results` – Maximum number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `fields` – Specific fields to return in results *(optional)*

    <Tip>
      Options to filter by place types and customize the returned fields and number of results.
    </Tip>

  </Accordion>
</AccordionGroup>
