>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/microsoft_teams.svg"
    alt="Microsoft Teams"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Microsoft Teams</h2>
</div>

Microsoft Teams integrates chat, video meetings, and file storage within Microsoft 365, providing virtual collaboration and communication for distributed teams.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Chats Get All Chats" icon="comments">
    Retrieves all Microsoft Teams chats a specified user is part of.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all Microsoft Teams chats a specified user is part of, supporting filtering, property selection, and pagination.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user_id` – The user ID *(required)*
    - `filter` – OData filter expression *(optional)*
    - `select` – Property selection *(optional)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `skip` – Number of results to skip *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Chats Get All Messages" icon="message">
    Retrieves all messages from a specified Microsoft Teams chat.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all messages from a specified Microsoft Teams chat using the Microsoft Graph API, automatically handling pagination; ensure `chat_id` is valid and OData expressions in `filter` or `select` are correct.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `chat_id` – The chat ID *(required)*
    - `filter` – OData filter expression *(optional)*
    - `select` – Property selection *(optional)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `skip` – Number of results to skip *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Meeting" icon="video">
    Schedule a new standalone Microsoft Teams online meeting.

    **Description:**
    Use to schedule a new standalone Microsoft Teams online meeting, i.e., one not linked to any calendar event.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `subject` – Meeting subject *(required)*
    - `start_time` – Meeting start time *(required)*
    - `end_time` – Meeting end time *(required)*
    - `participants` – List of participant email addresses *(optional)*
    - Additional meeting settings *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Chat Message" icon="message">
    Get a specific chat message.

    **Description:**
    Tool to get a specific chat message. Use after confirming chat_id and message_id.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `chat_id` – The chat ID *(required)*
    - `message_id` – The message ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Message Replies" icon="reply">
    List replies to a channel message.

    **Description:**
    Tool to list replies to a channel message. Use after obtaining team, channel, and message IDs.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `channel_id` – The channel ID *(required)*
    - `message_id` – The message ID *(required)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `skip` – Number of results to skip *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Team Members" icon="users">
    List members of a Microsoft Teams team.

    **Description:**
    Tool to list members of a Microsoft Teams team. Use when you need to retrieve the members of a specific team, for auditing or notifications.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `skip` – Number of results to skip *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Users" icon="users">
    List all users in the organization.

    **Description:**
    Tool to list all users in the organization. Use when you need to retrieve directory users with filtering, pagination, and field selection.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `filter` – OData filter expression *(optional)*
    - `select` – Property selection *(optional)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `skip` – Number of results to skip *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Search Messages" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Search Microsoft Teams messages using powerful KQL syntax.

    **Description:**
    Search Microsoft Teams messages using powerful KQL syntax. Supports sender (from:), date filters (sent:), attachments, and boolean logic. Works across all Teams chats and channels the user has access to. Examples: 'from:user@example.com AND sent>=2024-10-01', 'punchlist OR termination', 'sent>today-30 AND hasattachment:yes'

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – KQL search query *(required)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Teams Create Chat" icon="message-plus">
    Creates a new chat.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new chat; if a 'oneOnOne' chat with the specified members already exists, its details are returned, while 'group' chats are always newly created.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `chat_type` – Chat type (oneOnOne or group) *(required)*
    - `members` – List of member email addresses or IDs *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Teams Get Message" icon="message">
    Retrieves a specific message from a Microsoft Teams channel.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a specific message from a Microsoft Teams channel using its Team, Channel, and Message IDs.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `channel_id` – The channel ID *(required)*
    - `message_id` – The message ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Teams List Chat Messages" icon="comments">
    Retrieves messages from an existing Microsoft Teams chat or channel thread.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves messages (newest first) from an existing and accessible Microsoft Teams one-on-one chat, group chat, or channel thread, specified by `chat_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `chat_id` – The chat ID *(required)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `skip` – Number of results to skip *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Teams List People" icon="users">
    Retrieves a list of people relevant to a specified user.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of people relevant to a specified user from Microsoft Graph, noting the `search` parameter is only effective if `user_id` is 'me'.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user_id` – The user ID (use 'me' for current user) *(required)*
    - `search` – Search query (only works if user_id is 'me') *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Teams Post Channel Message" icon="paper-plane">
    Posts a new text or HTML message to a specified channel.

    **Description:**
    Posts a new text or HTML message to a specified channel in a Microsoft Teams team.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `channel_id` – The channel ID *(required)*
    - `content` – Message content *(required)*
    - `content_type` – Content type (text or html) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Teams Post Chat Message" icon="paper-plane">
    Sends a message to a specified Microsoft Teams chat.

    **Description:**
    Sends a non-empty message (text or HTML) to a specified, existing Microsoft Teams chat; content must be valid HTML if `content_type` is 'html'.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `chat_id` – The chat ID *(required)*
    - `content` – Message content *(required)*
    - `content_type` – Content type (text or html) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Channel Message" icon="pencil">
    Update a message in a channel.

    **Description:**
    Tool to update a message in a channel. Use when you need to modify an existing channel message after confirming channel and message IDs.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `team_id` – The team ID *(required)*
    - `channel_id` – The channel ID *(required)*
    - `message_id` – The message ID *(required)*
    - `content` – Updated message content *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Chat Message" icon="pencil">
    Update a specific message in a chat.

    **Description:**
    Tool to update a specific message in a chat. Use when you need to correct or modify a sent chat message.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `chat_id` – The chat ID *(required)*
    - `message_id` – The message ID *(required)*
    - `content` – Updated message content *(required)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

  <img

    alt="Monday.com"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Monday.com</h2>
</div>

monday.com is a customizable work management platform for project planning, collaboration, and automation, supporting agile, sales, marketing, and more.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Archive Item" icon="archive">
    Archive an existing Monday.com item.

    **Description:**
    Archives an existing Monday.com item, moving it from active board views to the archive where it can be potentially restored.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `item_id` – The item ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Change Simple Column Value" icon="pencil">
    Change a specific column's value for a Monday.com item.

    **Description:**
    Changes a specific column's value for a Monday.com item using a simple string, suitable for Text, Status, or Dropdown columns; can create new labels if `create_labels_if_missing` is true for Status/Dropdown columns.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `item_id` – The item ID *(required)*
    - `column_id` – The column ID *(required)*
    - `value` – The new column value *(required)*
    - `create_labels_if_missing` – Create labels if missing (for Status/Dropdown) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Item" icon="plus">
    Create a new item on a Monday.com board.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new item on a Monday.com board, optionally assigning it to a group and setting column values.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `board_id` – The board ID *(required)*
    - `item_name` – The item name *(required)*
    - `group_id` – The group ID *(optional)*
    - `column_values` – Column values to set *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Update" icon="note-sticky">
    Create a new update for an item or reply to an existing update.

    **Description:**
    Tool to create a new update for an item or reply to an existing update. Use after determining the target item or update to comment on.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `item_id` – The item ID *(required)*
    - `body` – Update content *(required)*
    - `parent_update_id` – Parent update ID (for replies) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Item" icon="trash">
    Permanently delete an existing Monday.com item.

    **Description:**
    Permanently deletes an existing Monday.com item; this action is irreversible via the API.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `item_id` – The item ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Update" icon="trash">
    Delete an update by its ID.

    **Description:**
    Tool to delete an update by its ID. Use when an update is no longer relevant. Use after confirming deletion is irreversible.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `update_id` – The update ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Duplicate Item" icon="copy">
    Duplicate an item on a Monday.com board.

    **Description:**
    Duplicates an item on a Monday.com board, optionally including its updates.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `item_id` – The item ID *(required)*
    - `include_updates` – Include item updates in duplication *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Me" icon="user">
    Fetch the current authenticated user's profile and permissions.

    **Description:**
    Tool to fetch the current authenticated user's profile and permissions. Use when you need to retrieve user metadata before performing other operations.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None—returns current user information*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Tags" icon="tags">
    Retrieve tags from the account.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve tags from the account. Use when you need to list all tags or filter by specific IDs.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `tag_ids` – List of tag IDs to filter *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Updates" icon="comments">
    Retrieve updates for a specific item.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve updates for a specific item. Use when you need to fetch the conversation history tied to an item.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `item_id` – The item ID *(required)*
    - `limit` – Number of updates to retrieve *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Board Items" icon="list">
    Retrieve ID, name, and state for all items on a specified board.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves ID, name, and state for all items on a specified Monday.com board.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `board_id` – The board ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Boards" icon="table">
    Retrieve a list of boards from a Monday.com account.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of boards from a Monday.com account, supporting pagination and filtering by state.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `state` – Filter by board state *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Number of boards to retrieve *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Groups" icon="layer-group">
    Retrieve all groups of a specified board.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve all groups of a specified board. Use when you need to list groups on a board after confirming its board ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `board_id` – The board ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Items" icon="list">
    Retrieve specified subitems from Monday.com using their IDs.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves specified subitems from Monday.com using their IDs, returning the raw JSON response.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `item_ids` – List of item IDs *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Users" icon="users">
    Retrieve a list of users from Monday.com.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of users from Monday.com; an empty user list in the response 'data' field does not signify action failure.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of users to retrieve *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Move Item To Board" icon="arrow-right">
    Move a Monday.com item to a specified board and group.

    **Description:**
    Moves a Monday.com item to a specified board and group; requires the item, target board, and target group to exist.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `item_id` – The item ID *(required)*
    - `board_id` – The target board ID *(required)*
    - `group_id` – The target group ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Move Item To Group" icon="arrow-right">
    Move an item to a different group on the same board.

    **Description:**
    Moves an item to a different group on the same Monday.com board; the item and group must exist.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `item_id` – The item ID *(required)*
    - `group_id` – The target group ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Item" icon="pencil">
    Update an existing item's column value on Monday.com.

    **Description:**
    Tool to update an existing item's column value on Monday.com. Use when setting complex column types like Timeline or People.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `item_id` – The item ID *(required)*
    - `column_id` – The column ID *(required)*
    - `value` – The column value (JSON format for complex types) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Update" icon="pencil">
    Edit an existing update's content.

    **Description:**
    Tool to edit an existing update's content. Use when you need to correct or change a previously posted update.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `update_id` – The update ID *(required)*
    - `body` – Updated content *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update User" icon="user-pen">
    Update a user on Monday.com.

    **Description:**
    Tool to update a user on Monday.com. Use when changing profile attributes like name, email, or department; ensure user ID is valid.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user_id` – The user ID *(required)*
    - `name` – User name *(optional)*
    - `email` – User email *(optional)*
    - `department` – User department *(optional)*
    - Additional user attributes *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-notion.com"
    alt="Notion"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Notion</h2>
</div>

Notion centralizes notes, docs, wikis, and tasks in a unified workspace, letting teams build custom workflows for collaboration and knowledge management.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Append Block Children" icon="plus">
    Appends raw Notion API blocks to parent.

    **Description:**
    Appends raw Notion API blocks to parent. CRITICAL: Text content limited to 2000 chars per text.content field. Use for: Advanced blocks (tables, databases), pre-built block objects, complex nested structures. REQUIRES exact Notion block schema - each block MUST have 'object':'block' and 'type'. Text blocks MUST use rich_text arrays with type 'text' and content structure. Common errors include invalid content structure or missing required fields.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `block_id` – The parent block ID *(required)*
    - `children` – Array of block objects *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Archive Notion Page" icon="archive">
    Archive or unarchive a specified Notion page.

    **Description:**
    Archives (moves to trash) or unarchives (restores from trash) a specified Notion page.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `page_id` – The page ID *(required)*
    - `archived` – Archive status (true to archive, false to unarchive) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Comment" icon="comment">
    Add a comment to a Notion page or discussion thread.

    **Description:**
    Adds a comment to a Notion page (via `parent_page_id`) OR to an existing discussion thread (via `discussion_id`); cannot create new discussion threads on specific blocks (inline comments).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `parent_page_id` – The page ID (for page comments) *(optional)*
    - `discussion_id` – The discussion ID (for thread replies) *(optional)*
    - `rich_text` – Comment content *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Notion Page" icon="file-plus">
    Create a new empty page in a Notion workspace.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new empty page in a Notion workspace under a specified parent page or database. PREREQUISITES: - Parent page/database must exist and be accessible in your Notion workspace - Use search_pages or list_databases first to obtain valid parent IDs LIMITATIONS: - Cannot create root-level pages (must have a parent) - May encounter conflicts if creating pages too quickly - Title-based parent search is less reliable than using UUIDs

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `parent_id` – The parent page or database ID *(required)*
    - `title` – Page title *(optional)*
    - `properties` – Page properties *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Block" icon="trash">
    Archive a Notion block, page, or database.

    **Description:**
    Archives a Notion block, page, or database using its ID, which sets its 'archived' property to true (like moving to \"Trash\" in the UI) and allows it to be restored later.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `block_id` – The block, page, or database ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Duplicate Page" icon="copy">
    Duplicate a Notion page with all its content.

    **Description:**
    Duplicates a Notion page, including all its content, properties, and nested blocks, under a specified parent page or workspace.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `page_id` – The page ID to duplicate *(required)*
    - `parent_id` – The parent page ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Block Contents" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve child blocks for a given parent block or page.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a paginated list of direct, first-level child block objects along with contents for a given parent Notion block or page ID; use block IDs from the response for subsequent calls to access deeply nested content.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `block_id` – The parent block or page ID *(required)*
    - `page_size` – Number of results per page *(optional)*
    - `start_cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Data" icon="database">
    Fetch Notion items (pages and/or databases) from the workspace.

    **Description:**
    Fetches Notion items (pages and/or databases) from the Notion workspace, use this to get minimal data about the items in the workspace with a query or list all items in the workspace with minimal data

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query *(optional)*
    - `filter` – Filter criteria *(optional)*
    - `page_size` – Number of results per page *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Database" icon="database">
    Fetch a Notion database's structural metadata.

    **Description:**
    Fetches a Notion database's structural metadata (properties, title, etc.) via its `database_id`, not the data entries; `database_id` must reference an existing database.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `database_id` – The database ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Row" icon="table">
    Retrieve a Notion database row's properties and metadata.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a Notion database row's properties and metadata; use fetch_block_contents for page content blocks.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `page_id` – The row (page) ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get About User" icon="user">
    Retrieve detailed information about a specific Notion user.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information about a specific Notion user, such as their name, avatar, and email, based on their unique user ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user_id` – The user ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Page Property Action" icon="file-lines">
    Get a specific property from a Notion page.

    **Description:**
    Call this to get a specific property from a Notion page when you have a valid `page_id` and `property_id`; handles pagination for properties returning multiple items.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `page_id` – The page ID *(required)*
    - `property_id` – The property ID *(required)*
    - `start_cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*
    - `page_size` – Number of results per page *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Insert Row Database" icon="plus">
    Create a new page (row) in a specified Notion database.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new page (row) in a specified Notion database.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `database_id` – The database ID *(required)*
    - `properties` – Row properties *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Users" icon="users">
    Retrieve a paginated list of users from the Notion workspace.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a paginated list of users (excluding guests) from the Notion workspace; the number of users returned per page may be less than the requested `page_size`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `page_size` – Number of users per page *(optional)*
    - `start_cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Query Database" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Query a Notion database to retrieve pages (rows).

    **Description:**
    Queries a Notion database to retrieve pages (rows). In Notion, databases are collections where each row is a page and columns are properties. Returns paginated results with metadata.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `database_id` – The database ID *(required)*
    - `page_size` – Number of results per page *(optional)*
    - `start_cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Query Database With Filter" icon="filter">
    Query a Notion database with server-side filtering, sorting, and pagination.

    **Description:**
    Tool to query a Notion database with server-side filtering, sorting, and pagination. Use when you need to retrieve a subset of rows by property, date, status, or other conditions.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `database_id` – The database ID *(required)*
    - `filter` – Filter criteria *(optional)*
    - `sorts` – Sort criteria *(optional)*
    - `page_size` – Number of results per page *(optional)*
    - `start_cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Search Notion Page" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Search Notion pages and databases by title.

    **Description:**
    Searches Notion pages and databases by title; an empty query lists all accessible items, useful for discovering IDs or as a fallback when a specific query yields no results.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query (empty to list all) *(optional)*
    - `filter` – Filter criteria *(optional)*
    - `page_size` – Number of results per page *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Block" icon="pencil">
    Update existing Notion block's text content.

    **Description:**
    Updates existing Notion block's text content. ⚠️ CRITICAL: Content limited to 2000 chars. Cannot change block type or archive blocks. Content exceeding 2000 chars will fail with validation error. For longer content, split across multiple blocks using add_multiple_page_content.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `block_id` – The block ID *(required)*
    - `rich_text` – Updated text content (max 2000 chars) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Page" icon="pencil">
    Update page properties, icon, cover, or archive status.

    **Description:**
    Update page properties, icon, cover, or archive status. Requires at least one update parameter.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `page_id` – The page ID *(required)*
    - `properties` – Page properties to update *(optional)*
    - `icon` – Page icon *(optional)*
    - `cover` – Page cover *(optional)*
    - `archived` – Archive status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Row Database" icon="pencil">
    Update a Notion database row (page) by its UUID.

    **Description:**
    Updates a Notion database row (page) by its UUID. Common issues: (1) Use UUID from page URL, not the full URL, (2) Ensure page is shared with integration, (3) Match property names exactly as in database, (4) Use 'status' type for Status properties, not 'select', (5) Retry on 409 Conflict errors (concurrent updates). Supports updating properties, icon, cover, or archiving the row.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `page_id` – The row (page) UUID *(required)*
    - `properties` – Properties to update *(required)*
    - `icon` – Row icon *(optional)*
    - `cover` – Row cover *(optional)*
    - `archived` – Archive status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/outlook.svg"
    alt="Outlook"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Outlook</h2>
</div>

Outlook is Microsoft's email and calendaring platform integrating contacts, tasks, and scheduling, enabling users to manage communications and events in a unified workspace.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Calendar Create Event" icon="calendar-plus">
    Create a new Outlook calendar event.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new Outlook calendar event, ensuring `start_datetime` is chronologically before `end_datetime`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `subject` – Event subject *(required)*
    - `start_datetime` – Event start date and time *(required)*
    - `end_datetime` – Event end date and time *(required)*
    - `attendees` – List of attendee email addresses *(optional)*
    - `location` – Event location *(optional)*
    - `body` – Event description *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Contact" icon="user-plus">
    Create a new contact in Outlook.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new contact in a Microsoft Outlook user's contacts folder.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `given_name` – First name *(optional)*
    - `surname` – Last name *(optional)*
    - `email_addresses` – List of email addresses *(optional)*
    - `phone_numbers` – List of phone numbers *(optional)*
    - Additional contact fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Draft" icon="file-pen">
    Create an Outlook email draft.

    **Description:**
    Creates an Outlook email draft with subject, body, recipients, and an optional attachment. Supports creating drafts as part of existing conversation threads by specifying a conversationId; attachments require a name, mimetype, and content.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `subject` – Email subject *(required)*
    - `body` – Email body content *(required)*
    - `to_email` – Recipient email addresses *(required)*
    - `cc` – CC recipients *(optional)*
    - `bcc` – BCC recipients *(optional)*
    - `conversation_id` – Conversation ID for threading *(optional)*
    - `attachments` – List of attachments *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Draft Reply" icon="reply">
    Create a draft reply to an existing message.

    **Description:**
    Creates a draft reply in the specified user's Outlook mailbox to an existing message (identified by a valid `message_id`), optionally including a `comment` and CC/BCC recipients.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `message_id` – The message ID to reply to *(required)*
    - `comment` – Reply content *(optional)*
    - `cc` – CC recipients *(optional)*
    - `bcc` – BCC recipients *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Contact" icon="trash">
    Permanently delete an existing contact.

    **Description:**
    Permanently deletes an existing contact, using its `contact_id` (obtainable via 'List User Contacts' or 'Get Contact'), from the Outlook contacts of the user specified by `user_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID *(required)*
    - `user_id` – The user ID (defaults to 'me') *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Event" icon="trash">
    Delete an existing calendar event.

    **Description:**
    Deletes an existing calendar event, identified by its unique `event_id`, from a specified user's Microsoft Outlook calendar, with an option to send cancellation notifications to attendees.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_id` – The event ID *(required)*
    - `send_cancellation` – Send cancellation to attendees *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Calendar View" icon="calendar">
    Get events active during a time window.

    **Description:**
    Get events ACTIVE during a time window (includes multi-day events). Use for \"what's on my calendar today/this week\" or availability checks. Returns events overlapping the time range. For keyword search or filters by category, use OUTLOOK_LIST_EVENTS instead.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `start_datetime` – Start of time window *(required)*
    - `end_datetime` – End of time window *(required)*
    - `calendar_id` – Calendar ID (defaults to primary) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Contact" icon="user">
    Retrieve a specific Outlook contact.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a specific Outlook contact by its `contact_id` from the contacts of a specified `user_id` (defaults to 'me' for the authenticated user).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID *(required)*
    - `user_id` – The user ID (defaults to 'me') *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Event" icon="calendar">
    Retrieve full details of a specific calendar event.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves the full details of a specific calendar event by its ID from a user's Outlook calendar, provided the event exists.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_id` – The event ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Message" icon="envelope">
    Retrieve a specific email message by ID.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a specific email message by its ID from the specified user's Outlook mailbox. Use the 'select' parameter to include specific fields like 'internetMessageHeaders' for filtering automated emails.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `message_id` – The message ID *(required)*
    - `select` – Fields to include *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Schedule" icon="clock">
    Retrieve free/busy schedule information.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves free/busy schedule information for specified email addresses within a defined time window.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `schedules` – List of email addresses *(required)*
    - `start_time` – Start of time window *(required)*
    - `end_time` – End of time window *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Calendars" icon="calendar">
    List calendars in the signed-in user's mailbox.

    **Description:**
    Tool to list calendars in the signed-in user's mailbox. Use when you need to retrieve calendars with optional OData queries.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `filter` – OData filter expression *(optional)*
    - `select` – Property selection *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Contacts" icon="users">
    Retrieve a user's Microsoft Outlook contacts.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a user's Microsoft Outlook contacts, from the default or a specified contact folder.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `folder_id` – Contact folder ID *(optional)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `skip` – Number of results to skip *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Events" icon="calendar">
    Retrieve events from a user's Outlook calendar.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves events from a user's Outlook calendar via Microsoft Graph API. Supports primary/secondary/shared calendars, pagination, filtering, property selection, sorting, and timezone specification. Use calendar_id to access non-primary calendars.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `calendar_id` – Calendar ID (defaults to primary) *(optional)*
    - `filter` – OData filter expression *(optional)*
    - `select` – Property selection *(optional)*
    - `orderby` – Sort order *(optional)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Messages" icon="envelope">
    Retrieve a list of email messages from a mail folder.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of email messages from a specified mail folder in an Outlook mailbox, with options for filtering (including by conversationId to get all messages in a thread), pagination, and sorting; ensure 'user_id' and 'folder' are valid, and all date/time strings are in ISO 8601 format.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `folder` – Mail folder (e.g., 'inbox', 'sentitems') *(optional)*
    - `filter` – OData filter expression *(optional)*
    - `conversation_id` – Filter by conversation ID *(optional)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `skip` – Number of results to skip *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Reminders" icon="bell">
    Retrieve reminders for events within a time range.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve reminders for events occurring within a specified time range. Use when you need to see upcoming reminders between two datetimes.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `start_datetime` – Start of time range *(required)*
    - `end_datetime` – End of time range *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Move Message" icon="arrow-right">
    Move a message to another folder.

    **Description:**
    Move a message to another folder within the specified user's mailbox. This creates a new copy of the message in the destination folder and removes the original message.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `message_id` – The message ID *(required)*
    - `destination_folder_id` – The destination folder ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Query Emails" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Query Outlook emails with custom OData filters.

    **Description:**
    Primary tool for querying Outlook emails with custom OData filters. Build precise server-side filters for dates, read status, importance, subjects, attachments, and conversations. Best for structured queries on message metadata. Returns up to 100 messages per request with pagination support. Server-side filters include: dates, importance, isRead, hasAttachments, subjects, conversationId. CRITICAL: Always check response pagination metadata for additional results.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `filter` – OData filter expression *(required)*
    - `select` – Property selection *(optional)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `skip` – Number of results to skip *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Reply Email" icon="reply">
    Send a plain text reply to an Outlook email.

    **Description:**
    Sends a plain text reply to an Outlook email message, identified by `message_id`, allowing optional CC and BCC recipients.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `message_id` – The message ID to reply to *(required)*
    - `comment` – Reply content *(required)*
    - `cc` – CC recipients *(optional)*
    - `bcc` – BCC recipients *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Search Messages" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Search Outlook messages using powerful KQL syntax.

    **Description:**
    Search Outlook messages using powerful KQL syntax. Supports sender (from:), recipient (to:, cc:), subject, date filters (received:, sent:), attachments, and boolean logic. Only works with Microsoft 365/Enterprise accounts (no @hotmail.com/@outlook.com). Examples: 'from:user@example.com AND received>=2025-10-01', 'to:info@jcdn.nl AND subject:invoice', 'received>today-30 AND hasattachment:yes'

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – KQL search query *(required)*
    - `top` – Number of results to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Send Draft" icon="paper-plane">
    Send an existing draft message.

    **Description:**
    Tool to send an existing draft message. Use after creating a draft when you want to deliver it to recipients immediately. Example: Send a draft message with ID 'AAMkAG…'.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `message_id` – The draft message ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Send Email" icon="paper-plane">
    Send an email with subject, body, and recipients.

    **Description:**
    Sends an email with subject, body, recipients, and an optional attachment via Microsoft Graph API. Supports comma-separated email addresses in the to_email field for multiple recipients. Attachments require a non-empty file with valid name and mimetype.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `subject` – Email subject *(required)*
    - `body` – Email body content *(required)*
    - `to_email` – Recipient email addresses (comma-separated) *(required)*
    - `cc` – CC recipients *(optional)*
    - `bcc` – BCC recipients *(optional)*
    - `attachments` – List of attachments *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Calendar Event" icon="pencil">
    Update specified fields of an existing calendar event.

    **Description:**
    Updates specified fields of an existing Outlook calendar event.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `event_id` – The event ID *(required)*
    - `subject` – Updated subject *(optional)*
    - `start_datetime` – Updated start time *(optional)*
    - `end_datetime` – Updated end time *(optional)*
    - `location` – Updated location *(optional)*
    - `body` – Updated description *(optional)*
    - Additional event fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Contact" icon="pencil">
    Update an existing Outlook contact.

    **Description:**
    Updates an existing Outlook contact, identified by `contact_id` for the specified `user_id`, requiring at least one other field to be modified.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID *(required)*
    - `given_name` – Updated first name *(optional)*
    - `surname` – Updated last name *(optional)*
    - `email_addresses` – Updated email addresses *(optional)*
    - `phone_numbers` – Updated phone numbers *(optional)*
    - Additional contact fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Email" icon="pencil">
    Update specified properties of an existing email message.

    **Description:**
    Updates specified properties of an existing email message; `message_id` must identify a valid message within the specified `user_id`'s mailbox.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `message_id` – The message ID *(required)*
    - `is_read` – Read status *(optional)*
    - `flag` – Flag status *(optional)*
    - `categories` – Message categories *(optional)*
    - Additional message properties *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-pagerduty.com"
    alt="PagerDuty"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>PagerDuty</h2>
</div>

Integrate PagerDuty to manage incidents, schedules, and alerts directly from your application.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Create Incident Record" icon="plus">
    Create a new incident in PagerDuty.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new incident in PagerDuty with specified details and assignments. Use this endpoint when an event requires immediate attention from on-call teams. It supports comprehensive incident documentation, including priority, urgency, and conference bridge information. The 'incident_key' parameter helps prevent duplicate incidents, crucial for maintaining a clean incident list.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `title` – Incident title *(required)*
    - `service_id` – Service ID *(required)*
    - `priority_id` – Priority ID *(optional)*
    - `urgency` – Urgency level *(optional)*
    - `incident_key` – Unique key to prevent duplicates *(optional)*
    - `body` – Incident description *(optional)*
    - `assignments` – List of assignments *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Incident List" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of incidents from PagerDuty.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of incidents from PagerDuty based on specified criteria. This endpoint allows users to fetch multiple incidents, making it useful for incident management, reporting, and analysis. It supports filtering by status and date range, as well as pagination for handling large result sets. The endpoint is particularly valuable for obtaining an overview of recent or ongoing incidents, tracking incident trends, or integrating PagerDuty incident data into external systems or dashboards.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `statuses` – Filter by status *(optional)*
    - `since` – Start date for filtering *(optional)*
    - `until` – End date for filtering *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `offset` – Pagination offset *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Priorities List" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of existing priorities in PagerDuty.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of existing priorities in the PagerDuty system, ordered from most severe to least severe. This endpoint should be used when you need to obtain information about the current priority levels configured in your PagerDuty account. It's particularly useful for integrations that need to reference or display priority information, or for administrators who want to review the existing priority structure.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None—returns all priorities*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Related Change Events For Incident" icon="clock">
    Retrieve change events related to a specific incident.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of change events related to a specific incident in PagerDuty. This endpoint is used to gather contextual information about changes or updates associated with an incident, which can be crucial for understanding its progression and resolution. It provides insights into actions taken, system modifications, or other relevant events that occurred in connection with the incident.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Related Incidents By Id" icon="link">
    Retrieve incidents potentially related to a specified incident.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of incidents that are potentially related to a specified incident in PagerDuty. This endpoint utilizes machine learning algorithms to identify and return incidents that may be connected or similar to the given incident. It's particularly useful for incident management teams to gain a broader context of ongoing issues, identify patterns, and potentially streamline resolution processes.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Alerts By Incident Id" icon="bell">
    Retrieve all alerts associated with a specific incident.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all alerts associated with a specific incident in PagerDuty. This endpoint allows users to fetch detailed information about the notifications and alerts that were triggered as part of an incident's lifecycle. It is particularly useful for incident postmortems, auditing purposes, or understanding the notification flow during an incident.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Incident Log Entries By Id" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve all log entries associated with a specific incident.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all log entries associated with a specific incident in PagerDuty. This endpoint provides a comprehensive history of actions, notifications, and status changes related to the incident. It should be used when detailed information about the lifecycle of an incident is needed, such as for post-incident reviews, auditing, or tracking the incident resolution process. The endpoint returns log entries in chronological order, allowing users to trace the incident's progression from creation to resolution.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Post Incident Note Using Id" icon="note-sticky">
    Add a new note to an existing incident.

    **Description:**
    Adds a new note to an existing incident in PagerDuty. This endpoint allows users to append additional information, updates, or comments to a specific incident identified by its unique ID. It's particularly useful for documenting the progress of incident resolution, sharing important observations, or recording actions taken. The note content can include any text relevant to the incident management process, helping teams collaborate and maintain a clear record of the incident's timeline and handling.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*
    - `content` – Note content *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Post Incident Status Update" icon="message">
    Post a status update for a specific incident.

    **Description:**
    Posts a status update for a specific incident in PagerDuty. This endpoint allows you to add new information or progress reports to an ongoing incident, keeping stakeholders informed about the current state of the issue. It supports both simple text updates and more detailed custom HTML email updates. Use this when you need to communicate important changes, actions taken, or any relevant information about the incident to the team or stakeholders.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*
    - `message` – Status update message *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Business Service Impacts" icon="chart-line">
    Retrieve the impacts of an incident on business services.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves the impacts of a specific incident on business services within PagerDuty. This endpoint allows users to assess the scope and severity of an ongoing incident by providing detailed information about which business services are affected and to what extent. It should be used when there's a need to understand the broader implications of an incident across the organization's critical operations.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Incident By Incident Id" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve detailed information about a specific incident.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information about a specific incident in PagerDuty using its unique identifier. This endpoint allows users to access comprehensive data about an individual incident, including its current status, assigned responders, and related metadata. It is particularly useful for tracking the progress of an ongoing incident, reviewing historical incident data, or integrating incident details into external systems or reports.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Incident Custom Fields" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of custom fields associated with incidents.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of custom fields associated with incidents in PagerDuty. Custom fields are additional data points that can be added to incidents to provide more detailed information tailored to specific organizational needs. This endpoint allows you to fetch all defined custom fields, which can be useful for understanding the structure of incident data, preparing for incident creation or updates, or auditing the current custom field configuration.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None—returns all custom fields*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Incident Custom Field Values" icon="list">
    Retrieve custom field values for a specific incident.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves the custom field values associated with a specific incident in PagerDuty. This endpoint allows users to access additional metadata that has been added to an incident, providing more context and enabling better incident management. It should be used when detailed information about an incident's custom fields is needed, such as for reporting, analysis, or integration with other systems. The endpoint returns only the custom field values and does not modify the incident or its fields.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Incident Field Options" icon="list">
    Retrieve available field options for a specific custom field.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves the available field options for a specific custom field associated with incidents in PagerDuty. This endpoint allows users to fetch the predefined set of values that can be assigned to a particular custom field, enabling efficient incident management and customization. Use this endpoint when you need to populate dropdowns, validate input, or understand the possible values for a custom field in your incident management workflow.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `field_id` – The custom field ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve List Of Services" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of services configured in PagerDuty.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of services configured in the PagerDuty account. This endpoint allows you to fetch details about various services set up for incident management and alerting. It's particularly useful for getting an overview of all services, their configurations, and associated teams or escalation policies. The endpoint supports filtering, sorting, and pagination to manage large sets of services efficiently.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `offset` – Pagination offset *(optional)*
    - `query` – Search query *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Maintenance Windows" icon="calendar">
    Retrieve a list of maintenance windows.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of maintenance windows from the PagerDuty incident management platform. Maintenance windows are scheduled periods during which alerts and notifications for specified services are suppressed to allow for system maintenance or updates without triggering unnecessary incidents. This endpoint should be used to get an overview of all maintenance windows, their schedules, and affected services.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `offset` – Pagination offset *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Notes For Incident" icon="note-sticky">
    Retrieve all notes associated with a specific incident.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all notes associated with a specific incident in PagerDuty. This endpoint allows users to access the complete history of comments, updates, and additional information added to an incident throughout its lifecycle. It is particularly useful for reviewing the incident's progress, understanding the actions taken, and gathering context for post-incident analysis.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Oncall List" icon="users">
    Retrieve the current on-call information.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves the current on-call information for your PagerDuty account. This endpoint provides a comprehensive view of who is currently on-call across various schedules and escalation policies. It's particularly useful for getting an overview of your organization's current on-call status, identifying who is responsible for incident response at any given time, and planning team availability.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `schedule_ids` – Filter by schedule IDs *(optional)*
    - `escalation_policy_ids` – Filter by escalation policy IDs *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Past Incidents" icon="clock-rotate-left">
    Retrieve a list of past incidents related to a specific incident.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of past incidents related to a specific incident in PagerDuty. This endpoint allows users to explore the historical context of an incident by fetching previous occurrences or related issues. It's particularly useful for identifying recurring problems, analyzing incident patterns, and improving overall incident management processes. The endpoint should be used when investigating the root cause of an incident or when compiling reports on incident history.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Service By Id" icon="gear">
    Retrieve detailed information about a specific service.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information about a specific PagerDuty service using its unique identifier. This endpoint allows users to access configuration details, integration settings, and other relevant information for a particular service within their PagerDuty account. It's essential for managing and monitoring the status of individual services, which are core components in PagerDuty's incident management system.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `service_id` – The service ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Send Responder Requests For Incidents" icon="user-plus">
    Send responder requests for a specific incident.

    **Description:**
    This endpoint allows you to send responder requests for a specific incident in PagerDuty. It is used to request additional help or notify specific users or escalation policies about an ongoing incident that requires attention. The endpoint creates a new responder request associated with the incident identified by the {id} path parameter. It's particularly useful when you need to quickly engage additional resources or escalate an incident to ensure timely resolution.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*
    - `message` – Request message *(optional)*
    - `requester_id` – Requester user ID *(optional)*
    - `responders` – List of responder requests *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Alert In Incident" icon="pencil">
    Update the status of a specific alert within an incident.

    **Description:**
    Updates the status of a specific alert within an incident in PagerDuty. This endpoint allows you to modify an alert's status, primarily to mark it as resolved. It's crucial for managing the lifecycle of alerts and incidents in PagerDuty's incident management system. Use this when you need to programmatically update the state of an alert, typically as part of an automated incident resolution process or when integrating external systems with PagerDuty.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*
    - `alert_id` – The alert ID *(required)*
    - `status` – Alert status *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Incident By Id" icon="pencil">
    Modify various attributes of an existing incident.

    **Description:**
    The UpdateIncident endpoint allows you to modify various attributes of an existing incident in PagerDuty's incident management system. This PUT operation enables users to update incident status, priority, assignments, escalation levels, and other key properties. It's particularly useful for reflecting the current state of an incident, reassigning responsibilities, or adjusting the incident's urgency and escalation path.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*
    - `status` – Incident status *(optional)*
    - `priority_id` – Priority ID *(optional)*
    - `urgency` – Urgency level *(optional)*
    - `assignments` – List of assignments *(optional)*
    - Additional incident fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Incident Custom Field Values" icon="pencil">
    Update custom field values for a specific incident.

    **Description:**
    This endpoint updates custom field values for a specific incident in PagerDuty. It allows you to modify or add custom fields to provide additional context or information about the incident. The endpoint is particularly useful when you need to update incident metadata dynamically, such as changing the environment, priority, or any other custom attributes associated with the incident.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `incident_id` – The incident ID *(required)*
    - `custom_fields` – Custom field values to update *(required)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/pandadoc.svg"
    alt="PandaDoc"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>PandaDoc</h2>
</div>

PandaDoc offers document creation, e-signatures, and workflow automation, helping sales teams and businesses streamline proposals, contracts, and agreement processes.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Create Contact" icon="user-plus">
    Create a new contact in PandaDoc.

    **Description:**
    This tool creates a new contact in PandaDoc. It allows you to add a new contact with their personal and professional information to your PandaDoc account. The tool is completely independent and doesn't require any external resource IDs or dependencies.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Contact email address *(required)*
    - `first_name` – First name *(optional)*
    - `last_name` – Last name *(optional)*
    - `company` – Company name *(optional)*
    - `phone` – Phone number *(optional)*
    - Additional contact fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Or Update Contact" icon="user-pen">
    Create a new contact or update an existing one based on email.

    **Description:**
    This tool creates a new contact or updates an existing one in PandaDoc based on the email address. If a contact with the provided email exists, it will be updated; otherwise, a new contact will be created.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Contact email address *(required)*
    - `first_name` – First name *(optional)*
    - `last_name` – Last name *(optional)*
    - `company` – Company name *(optional)*
    - `phone` – Phone number *(optional)*
    - Additional contact fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Contact" icon="trash">
    Delete a contact from PandaDoc.

    **Description:**
    This tool allows you to delete a contact from your PandaDoc account. The action is permanent and cannot be undone.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `contact_id` – The contact ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Contacts" icon="users">
    List and search contacts in PandaDoc.

    **Description:**
    A tool to list and search contacts in PandaDoc. It retrieves a list of contacts with various options including filtering by email, search query, pagination, and shared status. All parameters are optional and it supports flexible queries to get contacts.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Filter by email address *(optional)*
    - `search` – Search query *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number for pagination *(optional)*
    - `count` – Number of results per page *(optional)*
    - `shared` – Filter by shared status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

Perplexity AI provides conversational AI models for generating human-like text responses.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Perplexity Ai Search" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Perform search queries using Perplexity AI.

    **Description:**
    Perplexity Ai Search interfaces with Perplexity AI to perform search queries and return responses from a range of models. This action manages requests to Perplexity AI and processes the resulting completions, which may include text, citations, and images based on selected models and settings.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query *(required)*
    - `model` – AI model to use *(optional)*
    - `search_domain` – Search domain filter *(optional)*
    - `return_images` – Include images in response *(optional)*
    - `return_related_questions` – Include related questions *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Pipedrive</h2>
</div>

Pipedrive is a sales management tool built around pipeline visualization, lead tracking, activity reminders, and automation to keep deals progressing.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Add A Call Log" icon="phone">
    Add a new call log.

    **Description:**
    Adds a new call log.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user_id` – User ID *(required)*
    - `deal_id` – Deal ID *(optional)*
    - `person_id` – Person ID *(optional)*
    - `org_id` – Organization ID *(optional)*
    - `duration` – Call duration in seconds *(optional)*
    - `outcome` – Call outcome *(optional)*
    - Additional call log fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Comment To A Note" icon="comment">
    Add a new comment to a note.

    **Description:**
    Adds a new comment to a note.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `note_id` – The note ID *(required)*
    - `content` – Comment content *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Deal" icon="plus">
    Add a new deal to Pipedrive.

    **Description:**
    Add a new deal to Pipedrive with any custom fields, which vary by account and are identified by long hash keys. Check dealFields for existing custom fields. For details, visit the tutorial on adding a deal.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `title` – Deal title *(required)*
    - `person_id` – Person ID *(optional)*
    - `org_id` – Organization ID *(optional)*
    - `stage_id` – Stage ID *(optional)*
    - `value` – Deal value *(optional)*
    - `currency` – Currency code *(optional)*
    - Custom fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Follower To A Deal" icon="user-plus">
    Add a follower to a deal.

    **Description:**
    Adds a follower to a deal.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `deal_id` – The deal ID *(required)*
    - `user_id` – The user ID to add as follower *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Follower To An Organization" icon="user-plus">
    Add a follower to an organization.

    **Description:**
    Adds a follower to an organization.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `org_id` – The organization ID *(required)*
    - `user_id` – The user ID to add as follower *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Follower To A Person" icon="user-plus">
    Add a follower to a person.

    **Description:**
    Adds a follower to a person.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `person_id` – The person ID *(required)*
    - `user_id` – The user ID to add as follower *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Follower To A Product" icon="user-plus">

    **Description:**
    Adds a follower to a product.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `product_id` – The product ID *(required)*
    - `user_id` – The user ID to add as follower *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Lead" icon="plus">
    Add a new lead to Pipedrive.

    **Description:**
    Pipedrive API lets you add leads linked to people or organizations and tags them with 'API' source. Custom fields from deals apply to leads and appear in responses if set. Details are in the tutorials for adding and updating leads.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `title` – Lead title *(required)*
    - `person_id` – Person ID *(optional)*
    - `org_id` – Organization ID *(optional)*
    - `label_ids` – Lead label IDs *(optional)*
    - Custom fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add An Activity" icon="calendar-plus">
    Add a new activity.

    **Description:**
    New activity added. Response includes `more_activities_scheduled_in_context` to show if more are planned with the same entity. See tutorial on adding activities [here](https://pipedrive.readme.io/docs/adding-an-activity).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `type` – Activity type *(required)*
    - `subject` – Activity subject *(required)*
    - `due_date` – Due date *(optional)*
    - `due_time` – Due time *(optional)*
    - `deal_id` – Deal ID *(optional)*
    - `person_id` – Person ID *(optional)*
    - `org_id` – Organization ID *(optional)*
    - Additional activity fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add An Installment Subscription" icon="plus">
    Add a new installment subscription.

    **Description:**
    Adds a new installment subscription. Note: Subscriptions endpoints may not be available on the company-specific base URL. To avoid 404s, this action overrides the default request behavior and uses the public API host (api.pipedrive.com) explicitly.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `deal_id` – Deal ID *(required)*
    - `installments` – Installment details *(required)*
    - `start_date` – Start date *(required)*
    - Additional subscription fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add An Organization" icon="plus">
    Add a new organization to Pipedrive.

    **Description:**
    Set up a new Pipedrive organization using custom fields with unique key hashes. Retrieve `organizationFields` for configuration. Check the linked tutorial for guidance.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `name` – Organization name *(required)*
    - `owner_id` – Owner user ID *(optional)*
    - `address` – Organization address *(optional)*
    - `phone` – Phone number *(optional)*
    - `email` – Email address *(optional)*
    - Custom fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Note" icon="note-sticky">
    Add a note to a deal, person, organization, lead, or project.

    **Description:**
    Add a note to a deal, person, organization, lead, or project in Pipedrive. At least one of deal_id, person_id, org_id, lead_id, or project_id must be provided.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `content` – Note content *(required)*
    - `deal_id` – Deal ID *(optional)*
    - `person_id` – Person ID *(optional)*
    - `org_id` – Organization ID *(optional)*
    - `lead_id` – Lead ID *(optional)*
    - `project_id` – Project ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Participant To A Deal" icon="user-plus">
    Add a participant to a deal.

    **Description:**
    Adds a participant to a deal.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `deal_id` – The deal ID *(required)*
    - `person_id` – The person ID to add as participant *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Person" icon="user-plus">
    Add a new contact in Pipedrive.

    **Description:**
    Add a new contact in Pipedrive with optional custom fields unique to each account found using the `personFields` endpoint. The endpoint also handles `data.marketing_status` for Campaigns product users.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `name` – Person name *(required)*
    - `email` – Email address *(optional)*
    - `phone` – Phone number *(optional)*
    - `org_id` – Organization ID *(optional)*
    - `owner_id` – Owner user ID *(optional)*
    - Custom fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Product" icon="plus">
    Add a new product to the Products inventory.

    **Description:**
    Adds a new product to the Products inventory. For more information, see the tutorial for <a href="https://pipedrive.readme.io/docs/adding-a-product" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">adding a product</a>.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `name` – Product name *(required)*
    - `code` – Product code *(optional)*
    - `unit` – Unit of measurement *(optional)*

    - Custom fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Product To A Deal" icon="plus">
    Add a product to a deal.

    **Description:**
    Adds a product to a deal, creating a new item called a deal-product.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `deal_id` – The deal ID *(required)*
    - `product_id` – The product ID *(required)*
    - `item_price` – Item price *(optional)*
    - `quantity` – Quantity *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Project" icon="plus">
    Add a new project.

    **Description:**
    Adds a new project. Note that you can supply additional custom fields along with the request that are not described here. These custom fields are different for each Pipedrive account and can be recognized by long hashes as keys.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**

    - `board_id` – Board ID *(optional)*
    - `owner_id` – Owner user ID *(optional)*
    - Custom fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add A Recurring Subscription" icon="plus">

    - Additional subscription fields *(optional)*

  <Accordion title="Add A Task" icon="plus">

    - `project_id` – The project ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Cancel A Recurring Subscription" icon="xmark">
    Cancel a recurring subscription.

    **Description:**
    Cancels a recurring subscription. This action attempts to cancel a recurring subscription via Subscriptions API. If Subscriptions endpoints are unavailable (404), it gracefully falls back to disabling all product attachments on the given deal (interpreting `id` as `deal_id`) to mimic cancellation behavior.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `subscription_id` – The subscription ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create An Organization Relationship" icon="link">
    Create an organization relationship.

    **Description:**
    Creates and returns an organization relationship.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `org_id` – Organization ID *(required)*
    - `type` – Relationship type *(required)*
    - `related_org_id` – Related organization ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete A Call Log" icon="trash">
    Delete a call log.

    **Description:**
    Deletes a call log. If there is an audio recording attached to it, it will also be deleted. The related activity will not be removed by this request. If you want to remove the related activities, please use the endpoint which is specific for activities.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `call_log_id` – The call log ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete A Comment Related To A Note" icon="trash">

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete A Deal" icon="trash">

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete A Product" icon="trash">

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete A Project" icon="trash">
    Mark a project as deleted.

    **Description:**
    Marks a project as deleted.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `project_id` – The project ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete A Subscription" icon="trash">
    Mark a subscription as deleted.

    **Description:**
    Marks an installment or a recurring subscription as deleted.

  <Accordion title="Search Item By Field" icon="magnifying-glass">

    **Description:**

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `field_key` – Field key to search *(required)*
    - `term` – Search term *(required)*
    - `return_item_ids` – Return item IDs flag *(optional)*

    **Description:**

    - `type` – Updated activity type *(optional)*
    - Additional activity fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update An Installment Subscription" icon="pencil">
    Update an installment subscription.

    **Description:**
    Updates an installment subscription. Note: Subscriptions endpoints may not be available on the company-specific base URL. To avoid 404s, this action overrides the default request behavior and uses multiple hosts along with a practical fallback to Deal Products when Subscriptions/Installments features are not accessible.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `subscription_id` – The subscription ID *(required)*
    - `installments` – Updated installment details *(optional)*
    - `start_date` – Updated start date *(optional)*
    - Additional subscription fields *(optional)*
