    - `board_id` – Updated board ID *(optional)*
    - `owner_id` – Updated owner ID *(optional)*
    - Custom fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update A Recurring Subscription" icon="pencil">
    Update a recurring subscription.

    **Description:**
    Updates a recurring subscription. Note: Some company hosts may not expose Subscriptions endpoints. This action will attempt multiple hosts and gracefully fall back to updating the product attached to a deal (v1) when applicable. In the fallback path, the request `id` is treated as the `product_attachment_id` and we locate the corresponding deal by scanning deal products.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `subscription_id` – The subscription ID *(required)*
    - `cycle_amount` – Updated cycle amount *(optional)*
    - `cycle_unit` – Updated cycle unit *(optional)*
    - `start_date` – Updated start date *(optional)*
    - Additional subscription fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update A Task" icon="pencil">
    Update a task.

    **Description:**
    Updates a task.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `text` – Updated task text *(optional)*
    - `due_date` – Updated due date *(optional)*
    - `assignee_id` – Updated assignee ID *(optional)*
    - `done` – Completion status *(optional)*
    - Additional task fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Task In Project Plan" icon="pencil">
    Update a task phase or group in a project.

    **Description:**
    Updates a task phase or group in a project.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `task_id` – The task ID *(required)*
    - `phase_id` – Phase ID *(optional)*
    - `group_id` – Group ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update The Product Attached To A Deal" icon="pencil">
    Update the details of a product attached to a deal.

    **Description:**
    Updates the details of the product that has been attached to a deal.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `product_attachment_id` – The product attachment ID *(required)*
    - `item_price` – Updated item price *(optional)*
    - `quantity` – Updated quantity *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

  <Accordion title="Add Opportunity Line Item" icon="plus">

    - `pricebook_entry_id` – The pricebook entry ID *(required)*

    - `account_id` – The account ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Clone Opportunity With Products" icon="copy">

    - `opportunity_id` – The opportunity ID to clone *(required)*
    - `include_products` – Include products in clone *(optional)*
    - `field_updates` – Field values to override *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `record_id` – The record ID to clone *(required)*

    - `field_updates` – Field values to override *(optional)*

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-shopify.com"
    alt="Shopify"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Shopify</h2>
</div>

Shopify is an e-commerce platform enabling merchants to create online stores, manage products, and process payments with themes, apps, and integrated marketing tools.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Create Customer" icon="user-plus">
    Create a new customer in Shopify.

    **Description:**
    Tool to create a new customer in Shopify. Use when you need to add a new customer record to the store.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Customer email address *(required)*
    - `first_name` – First name *(optional)*
    - `last_name` – Last name *(optional)*
    - `phone` – Phone number *(optional)*
    - `addresses` – Customer addresses *(optional)*
    - Additional customer fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Order" icon="plus">
    Create a new order in Shopify.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new order in Shopify, typically requiring line items; if `customer_id` is provided, it must correspond to an existing customer.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `line_items` – Order line items *(required)*
    - `customer_id` – Customer ID *(optional)*
    - `email` – Customer email *(optional)*
    - `shipping_address` – Shipping address *(optional)*
    - `billing_address` – Billing address *(optional)*
    - `financial_status` – Financial status *(optional)*
    - Additional order fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get All Customers" icon="users">
    Retrieve customer records from a Shopify store.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves customer records from a Shopify store, with options for filtering, selecting specific fields, and paginating through the results.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `fields` – Fields to retrieve *(optional)*
    - `since_id` – Return customers after this ID *(optional)*
    - `created_at_min` – Filter by minimum creation date *(optional)*
    - `created_at_max` – Filter by maximum creation date *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Collection By Id" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve a specific Shopify collection by ID.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a specific Shopify collection by its `collection_id`, optionally filtering returned data to specified `fields`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `collection_id` – The collection ID *(required)*
    - `fields` – Fields to retrieve *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Custom Collections" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of custom collections.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of custom collections from a Shopify store, optionally filtered by IDs, product ID, or handle.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `ids` – Collection IDs to filter *(optional)*
    - `product_id` – Filter by product ID *(optional)*
    - `handle` – Filter by handle *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Customer" icon="user">
    Retrieve detailed information for a specific customer.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information for a specific customer from a Shopify store, provided their valid and existing `customer_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `customer_id` – The customer ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Customer Orders" icon="list">
    Retrieve all orders for a specific customer.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all orders for a specific, existing customer in Shopify using their unique customer ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `customer_id` – The customer ID *(required)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `status` – Filter by order status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Order List" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of orders from Shopify.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of orders from Shopify using default API settings and filters.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `status` – Filter by order status *(optional)*
    - `financial_status` – Filter by financial status *(optional)*
    - `created_at_min` – Filter by minimum creation date *(optional)*
    - `created_at_max` – Filter by maximum creation date *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Ordersby Id" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve a specific Shopify order by ID.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a specific Shopify order by its unique ID, which must correspond to an existing order.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `order_id` – The order ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Product" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve details for an existing Shopify product.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves details for an existing Shopify product using its unique product ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `product_id` – The product ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Product Images" icon="image">
    Retrieve all images for a Shopify product.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all images for a Shopify product, specified by its `product_id` which must correspond to an existing product.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `product_id` – The product ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Products" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of products from a Shopify store.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of products from a Shopify store.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `fields` – Fields to retrieve *(optional)*
    - `vendor` – Filter by vendor *(optional)*
    - `product_type` – Filter by product type *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Products In Collection" icon="list">
    Retrieve all products within a specified Shopify collection.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all products within a specified Shopify collection, requiring a valid `collection_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `collection_id` – The collection ID *(required)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Products Paginated" icon="list">
    List products with Shopify cursor-based pagination.

    **Description:**
    Tool to list products with Shopify cursor-based pagination. Use when iterating over large product catalogs via the Link header.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results per page *(optional)*
    - `cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*
    - `fields` – Fields to retrieve *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Order" icon="pencil">
    Update the phone number for an existing Shopify order.

    **Description:**
    Updates the phone number for an existing Shopify order, identified by its ID; pass `phone=None` to remove the current phone number.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `order_id` – The order ID *(required)*
    - `phone` – Updated phone number *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/slack.svg"
    alt="Slack"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Slack</h2>
</div>

Slack is a channel-based messaging platform. With Slack, people can work together more effectively, connect all their software tools and services, and find the information they need to do their best work — all within a secure, enterprise-grade environment.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Create A Reminder" icon="bell">
    Create a Slack reminder with specified text and time.

    **Description:**
    Creates a Slack reminder with specified text and time; time accepts Unix timestamps, seconds from now, or natural language (e.g., 'in 15 minutes', 'every Thursday at 2pm').

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `text` – Reminder text *(required)*
    - `time` – Reminder time (Unix timestamp, seconds from now, or natural language) *(required)*
    - `user` – User ID to create reminder for *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete A Slack Reminder" icon="trash">
    Delete an existing Slack reminder.

    **Description:**
    Deletes an existing Slack reminder, typically when it is no longer relevant or a task is completed; this operation is irreversible.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `reminder_id` – The reminder ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Conversation History" icon="clock-rotate-left">
    Fetch messages and events from a Slack conversation.

    **Description:**
    Fetches a chronological list of messages and events from a specified Slack conversation, accessible by the authenticated user/bot, with options for pagination and time range filtering.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel` – Channel ID *(required)*
    - `oldest` – Oldest message timestamp to include *(optional)*
    - `latest` – Latest message timestamp to include *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Number of messages to return *(optional)*
    - `cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Fetch Message Thread From A Conversation" icon="comments">
    Retrieve replies to a specific parent message.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves replies to a specific parent message in a Slack conversation, using the channel ID and the parent message's timestamp (`ts`).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel` – Channel ID *(required)*
    - `ts` – Parent message timestamp *(required)*
    - `limit` – Number of replies to return *(optional)*
    - `cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Find Channels" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Find channels in a Slack workspace.

    **Description:**
    Find channels in a Slack workspace by any criteria - name, topic, purpose, or description.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query *(optional)*
    - `name` – Channel name filter *(optional)*
    - `topic` – Topic filter *(optional)*
    - `purpose` – Purpose filter *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Find User By Email Address" icon="envelope">
    Retrieve Slack user by email address.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves the Slack user object for an active user by their registered email address; fails with 'users_not_found' if the email is unregistered or the user is inactive.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Email address *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Find Users" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Find users in a Slack workspace.

    **Description:**
    Find users in a Slack workspace by any criteria - email, name, display name, or other text. Includes optimized email lookup for exact email matches.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query *(optional)*
    - `email` – Email filter *(optional)*
    - `name` – Name filter *(optional)*
    - `display_name` – Display name filter *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Canvas" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve a specific Slack Canvas by ID.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a specific Slack Canvas by its ID, including its content and metadata.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `canvas_id` – The Canvas ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Reminder Information" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve detailed information for an existing Slack reminder.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information for an existing Slack reminder specified by its ID; this is a read-only operation.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `reminder_id` – The reminder ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Team Dnd Status" icon="moon">
    Retrieve a user's current Do Not Disturb status.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a user's current Do Not Disturb status.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user` – User ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get User Presence Info" icon="circle-check">
    Retrieve a Slack user's current real-time presence.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a Slack user's current real-time presence (e.g., 'active', 'away') to determine their availability, noting this action does not provide historical data or status reasons.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user` – User ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List All Channels" icon="list">
    List conversations available to the user.

    **Description:**
    Lists conversations available to the user with various filters and search options.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `types` – Conversation types to include *(optional)*
    - `exclude_archived` – Exclude archived channels *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List All Users" icon="users">
    Retrieve a paginated list of all users in a Slack workspace.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a paginated list of all users, including comprehensive details, profile information, status, and team memberships, in a Slack workspace; data may not be real-time.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*
    - `include_locale` – Include locale information *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Canvases" icon="list">
    List Slack Canvases with filtering options.

    **Description:**
    Lists Slack Canvases with filtering by channel, user, timestamp, and page-based pagination. Uses Slack's files.list API with types=canvas filter.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel` – Filter by channel ID *(optional)*
    - `user` – Filter by user ID *(optional)*
    - `ts_from` – Filter by minimum timestamp *(optional)*
    - `ts_to` – Filter by maximum timestamp *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Conversations" icon="list">
    List conversations accessible to a specified user.

    **Description:**
    List conversations (channels/DMs) accessible to a specified user (or the authenticated user if no user ID is provided), respecting shared membership for non-public channels.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user` – User ID *(optional)*
    - `types` – Conversation types to include *(optional)*
    - `exclude_archived` – Exclude archived conversations *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Reminders" icon="list">
    List all reminders for the authenticated user.

    **Description:**
    Lists all reminders with their details for the authenticated Slack user; returns an empty list if no reminders exist.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None required*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Lists Pinned Items In A Channel" icon="thumbtack">
    Retrieve all messages and files pinned to a channel.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves all messages and files pinned to a specified channel; the caller must have access to this channel.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel` – Channel ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Conversation Members List" icon="users">
    Retrieve a paginated list of active member IDs for a conversation.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a paginated list of active member IDs for a specified Slack public channel, private channel, direct message (DM), or multi-person direct message (MPIM).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel` – Channel ID *(required)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `cursor` – Pagination cursor *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Current User Dnd Status" icon="moon">
    Retrieve a Slack user's current Do Not Disturb status.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a Slack user's current Do Not Disturb (DND) status to determine their availability before interaction; any specified user ID must be a valid Slack user ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user` – User ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Detailed User Information" icon="user">
    Retrieve comprehensive information for a Slack user.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves comprehensive information for a valid Slack user ID, excluding message history and channel memberships.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user` – User ID *(required)*
    - `include_locale` – Include locale information *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve User Profile Information" icon="user">
    Retrieve profile information for a specified Slack user.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves profile information for a specified Slack user (defaults to the authenticated user if `user` ID is omitted); a provided `user` ID must be valid.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `user` – User ID *(optional)*
    - `include_labels` – Include labels *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Search All" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Search all messages and files in Slack.

    **Description:**
    Tool to search all messages and files. Use when you need unified content search across channels and files in one call.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query *(required)*
    - `sort` – Sort order *(optional)*
    - `count` – Number of results per page *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Search Messages" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Workspace-wide Slack message search with filters.

    **Description:**
    Workspace‑wide Slack message search with date ranges and filters. Use `query` modifiers (e.g., in:#channel, from:@user, before/after:YYYY-MM-DD), sorting (score/timestamp), and pagination.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query with modifiers *(required)*
    - `sort` – Sort order (score or timestamp) *(optional)*
    - `sort_dir` – Sort direction *(optional)*
    - `count` – Number of results per page *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Send Message" icon="paper-plane">
    Post a message to a Slack channel, DM, or private group.

    **Description:**
    Posts a message to a Slack channel, direct message, or private group; requires content via `text`, `blocks`, or `attachments`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `channel` – Channel ID *(required)*
    - `text` – Message text *(optional)*
    - `blocks` – Message blocks *(optional)*
    - `attachments` – Message attachments *(optional)*
    - `thread_ts` – Thread timestamp for replies *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-stripe.com"
    alt="Stripe"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Stripe</h2>
</div>

Stripe offers online payment infrastructure, fraud prevention, and APIs enabling businesses to accept and manage payments globally.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Cancel Subscription" icon="xmark">
    Cancel a customer's active Stripe subscription.

    **Description:**
    Cancels a customer's active Stripe subscription at the end of the current billing period, with options to invoice immediately for metered usage and prorate charges for unused time.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `subscription_id` – The subscription ID *(required)*
    - `invoice_now` – Invoice immediately for metered usage *(optional)*
    - `prorate` – Prorate charges for unused time *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Confirm Payment Intent" icon="check">
    Confirm a Stripe PaymentIntent to finalize a payment.

    **Description:**
    Confirms a Stripe PaymentIntent to finalize a payment; a `return_url` is necessary if the payment method requires customer redirection.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `payment_intent_id` – The PaymentIntent ID *(required)*
    - `return_url` – Return URL for customer redirection *(optional)*
    - `payment_method` – Payment method ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Checkout Session" icon="plus">
    Create a Stripe Checkout Session.

    **Description:**
    Tool to create a Stripe Checkout Session. Use when you need a secure, hosted URL to collect payments or subscriptions via Stripe Checkout.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `success_url` – Success redirect URL *(required)*
    - `cancel_url` – Cancel redirect URL *(required)*
    - `line_items` – Line items for checkout *(optional)*
    - `mode` – Checkout mode (payment or subscription) *(optional)*
    - `customer` – Customer ID *(optional)*
    - Additional checkout options *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Customer" icon="user-plus">
    Create a new customer in Stripe.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new customer in Stripe, required for creating charges or subscriptions; an email is highly recommended for customer communications.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `email` – Customer email address *(optional)*
    - `name` – Customer name *(optional)*
    - `phone` – Phone number *(optional)*
    - `description` – Customer description *(optional)*
    - `metadata` – Additional metadata *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Invoice" icon="file-invoice">
    Create a new draft Stripe invoice.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new draft Stripe invoice for a customer; use to revise an existing invoice, bill for a specific subscription (which must belong to the customer), or apply detailed customizations.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `customer` – Customer ID *(required)*
    - `subscription` – Subscription ID *(optional)*
    - `description` – Invoice description *(optional)*
    - `line_items` – Invoice line items *(optional)*
    - `auto_advance` – Auto-finalize invoice *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Payment Intent" icon="plus">
    Create a Stripe PaymentIntent to initiate payment processing.

    **Description:**
    Creates a Stripe PaymentIntent to initiate and process a customer's payment; using `application_fee_amount` for a connected account requires the `Stripe-Account` header.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `amount` – Payment amount in cents *(required)*
    - `currency` – Currency code *(required)*
    - `payment_method_types` – Payment method types *(optional)*
    - `customer` – Customer ID *(optional)*
    - `application_fee_amount` – Application fee amount *(optional)*
    - Additional payment options *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Refund" icon="rotate-left">
    Create a full or partial refund in Stripe.

    **Description:**
    Creates a full or partial refund in Stripe, targeting either a specific charge ID or a payment intent ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `charge` – Charge ID *(optional)*
    - `payment_intent` – PaymentIntent ID *(optional)*
    - `amount` – Refund amount in cents *(optional)*
    - `reason` – Refund reason *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Subscription" icon="plus">
    Create a new subscription for an existing Stripe customer.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new, highly configurable subscription for an existing Stripe customer, supporting multiple items, trials, discounts, and various billing/payment options.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `customer` – Customer ID *(required)*
    - `items` – Subscription items *(required)*
    - `trial_period_days` – Trial period days *(optional)*
    - `coupon` – Coupon ID *(optional)*
    - `payment_behavior` – Payment behavior *(optional)*
    - Additional subscription options *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Customer" icon="trash">
    Permanently delete an existing Stripe customer.

    **Description:**
    Permanently deletes an existing Stripe customer; this irreversible action also cancels their active subscriptions and removes all associated data.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `customer_id` – The customer ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Charges" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of Stripe charges.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of Stripe charges with filtering and pagination; use valid cursor IDs from previous responses for pagination, and note that charges are typically returned in reverse chronological order.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `starting_after` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `ending_before` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `customer` – Filter by customer ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Coupons" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of discount coupons.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of discount coupons from a Stripe account, supporting pagination via `limit`, `starting_after`, and `ending_before`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `starting_after` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `ending_before` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Customer Payment Methods" icon="credit-card">
    Retrieve payment methods for a given customer.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of payment methods for a given customer, supporting type filtering and pagination.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `customer` – Customer ID *(required)*
    - `type` – Payment method type filter *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `starting_after` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Customers" icon="users">
    Retrieve a list of Stripe customers.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of Stripe customers, with options to filter by email, creation date, or test clock, and support for pagination.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `starting_after` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `ending_before` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `email` – Filter by email *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Invoices" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of Stripe invoices.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of Stripe invoices, filterable by various criteria and paginatable using invoice ID cursors obtained from previous responses.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `starting_after` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `ending_before` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `customer` – Filter by customer ID *(optional)*
    - `status` – Filter by status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Payment Intents" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of Stripe PaymentIntents.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of Stripe PaymentIntents, optionally filtered and paginated using PaymentIntent IDs as cursors.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `starting_after` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `ending_before` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `customer` – Filter by customer ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Payment Links" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of payment links from Stripe.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of payment links from Stripe, sorted by creation date in descending order by default.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `starting_after` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `ending_before` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Products" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of Stripe products.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of Stripe products, with optional filtering and pagination; `starting_after`/`ending_before` cursors must be valid product IDs from a previous response.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `starting_after` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `ending_before` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `active` – Filter by active status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Refunds" icon="list">
    List Stripe refunds with filtering and pagination.

    **Description:**
    Lists Stripe refunds, sorted by creation date descending (newest first), with optional filtering by charge or payment_intent and pagination support.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `starting_after` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `ending_before` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `charge` – Filter by charge ID *(optional)*
    - `payment_intent` – Filter by PaymentIntent ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Shipping Rates" icon="truck">
    Retrieve a list of Stripe shipping rates.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of Stripe shipping rates, filterable by active status, creation date, and currency; useful for managing or displaying shipping options.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `starting_after` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `ending_before` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `active` – Filter by active status *(optional)*
    - `currency` – Filter by currency *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="List Subscriptions" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of Stripe subscriptions.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of Stripe subscriptions, optionally filtered by various criteria such as customer, price, status, collection method, and date ranges, with support for pagination.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `starting_after` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `ending_before` – Cursor for pagination *(optional)*
    - `customer` – Filter by customer ID *(optional)*
    - `status` – Filter by status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Charge" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve full details for an existing Stripe charge.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves full details for an existing Stripe charge using its unique ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `charge_id` – The charge ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Customer" icon="user">
    Retrieve detailed information for an existing Stripe customer.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information for an existing Stripe customer using their unique customer ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `customer_id` – The customer ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Payment Intent" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve a PaymentIntent by its ID.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a PaymentIntent by its ID; `client_secret` is required if a publishable API key is used.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `payment_intent_id` – The PaymentIntent ID *(required)*
    - `client_secret` – Client secret (if using publishable key) *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Refund" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve details for an existing Stripe refund.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves details for an existing Stripe refund using its unique `refund_id`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `refund_id` – The refund ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Retrieve Subscription" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve detailed information for an existing Stripe subscription.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves detailed information for an existing Stripe subscription using its unique ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `subscription_id` – The subscription ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Search Customers" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Retrieve customers matching a search query.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a list of Stripe customers matching a search query that adheres to Stripe's Search Query Language.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `query` – Search query *(required)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Customer" icon="pencil">
    Update an existing Stripe customer.

    **Description:**
    Updates an existing Stripe customer, identified by customer_id, with only the provided details; unspecified fields remain unchanged.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `customer_id` – The customer ID *(required)*
    - `email` – Updated email *(optional)*
    - `name` – Updated name *(optional)*
    - `phone` – Updated phone *(optional)*
    - `description` – Updated description *(optional)*
    - `metadata` – Updated metadata *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Payment Intent" icon="pencil">
    Update a Stripe PaymentIntent with new values.

    **Description:**
    Updates a Stripe PaymentIntent with new values for specified parameters; note that if `currency` is updated, `amount` might also be required, and certain updates (e.g., to `payment_method`) can necessitate re-confirmation by the customer.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `payment_intent_id` – The PaymentIntent ID *(required)*
    - `amount` – Updated amount *(optional)*
    - `currency` – Updated currency *(optional)*
    - `payment_method` – Updated payment method *(optional)*
    - `metadata` – Updated metadata *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Subscription" icon="pencil">
    Update an existing Stripe subscription.

    **Description:**
    Updates an existing, non-canceled Stripe subscription by its ID, ensuring all referenced entity IDs (e.g., prices, coupons) are valid and automatic tax liability is correctly specified if enabled.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `subscription_id` – The subscription ID *(required)*
    - `items` – Updated subscription items *(optional)*
    - `coupon` – Updated coupon *(optional)*
    - `proration_behavior` – Proration behavior *(optional)*
    - `metadata` – Updated metadata *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

SurveyMonkey is an online survey development platform that enables users to create, distribute, and analyze surveys for various purposes.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Get Collectors" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of collectors for a specific survey.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve a list of collectors for a specific survey. Use when you need collector URLs, counts, and statuses.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `survey_id` – The survey ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Contacts" icon="users">
    Retrieve a list of contacts.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve a list of contacts. Use after authenticating with SurveyMonkey. Call this to fetch all contacts associated with your account.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    *None required*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Responses" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of responses for a specific survey.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve a list of responses for a specific survey. Use when you need to browse or filter responses after confirming the survey ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `survey_id` – The survey ID *(required)*
    - `page` – Page number for pagination *(optional)*
    - `per_page` – Number of results per page *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Survey Details" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve metadata and counts for a specific survey.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve metadata and counts for a specific survey. Use after confirming the survey ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `survey_id` – The survey ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Surveys" icon="list">
    Retrieve a list of surveys.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve a list of surveys. Use when you need to enumerate or paginate through all surveys.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `page` – Page number for pagination *(optional)*
    - `per_page` – Number of results per page *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

<div
  style={{

  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/app-trello.com"

  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Trello</h2>
</div>

A web-based, kanban-style, list-making application.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Add Cards" icon="plus">
    Create a new card in a Trello list.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new card in a Trello list; `idList` is required, and if `idCardSource` is used, the source card must be accessible.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idList` – List ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Card name *(required)*
    - `desc` – Card description *(optional)*
    - `due` – Due date *(optional)*
    - `idCardSource` – Source card ID to copy from *(optional)*
    - Additional card fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Cards Actions Comments By Id Card" icon="comment">
    Add a new text comment to a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Adds a new text comment, which can include @mentions, to a Trello card specified by its ID; file attachments are not supported via this action.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `text` – Comment text *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Cards Checklist Check Item By Id Card By Id Checklist" icon="check">
    Add a new check item to an existing checklist.

    **Description:**
    Adds a new check item to an existing checklist on a specific Trello card.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Check item name *(required)*
    - `checked` – Checked status *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Cards Checklists By Id Card" icon="list-check">
    Add a checklist to a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Adds a checklist to a Trello card: use `value` to add a specific existing checklist, `idChecklistSource` to create a new checklist by copying an existing one (optionally using `name` for the new checklist's name), or `name` to create a new empty checklist from scratch.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Checklist name *(optional)*
    - `idChecklistSource` – Source checklist ID to copy *(optional)*
    - `value` – Existing checklist ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Cards Id Labels By Id Card" icon="tag">
    Add an existing label to a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Adds an existing label to a Trello card; `idCard` identifies the card and `value` is the ID of the label to add. Both card and label must already exist.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `value` – Label ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Cards Id Members By Id Card" icon="user-plus">
    Assign a Trello member to a card.

    **Description:**
    Assigns a Trello member to a specific Trello card by card ID (or short link) and member ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `value` – Member ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Cards Labels By Id Card" icon="tag">
    Add a label to an existing Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Adds a label to an existing Trello card (specified by `idCard`), defining the label by `name` and either `color` or the overriding `value` (which specifies color by name); a new label is created on the board if a matching one (by name/color combination) doesn't already exist.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Label name *(optional)*
    - `color` – Label color *(optional)*
    - `value` – Label color name *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Checklists" icon="plus">
    Create a new checklist on a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new checklist on a Trello card, either by name or by copying from `idChecklistSource`, targeting an `idCard` or `idBoard`; this action creates only the checklist structure, not its items.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – Card ID *(optional)*
    - `idBoard` – Board ID *(optional)*
    - `name` – Checklist name *(required)*
    - `idChecklistSource` – Source checklist ID to copy *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Checklists Check Items By Id Checklist" icon="check">
    Add a new check item to a checklist.

    **Description:**
    Adds a new check item to a specified Trello checklist; this action does not update existing check items.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Check item name *(required)*
    - `checked` – Checked status *(optional)*
    - `pos` – Position *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Lists Cards By Id List" icon="plus">
    Create a new card in a Trello list.

    **Description:**
    Creates a new card in a Trello list, which must be specified by an existing and accessible `idList`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idList` – The list ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Card name *(required)*
    - `desc` – Card description *(optional)*
    - `due` – Due date *(optional)*
    - Additional card fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Convert Checklist Item To Card" icon="arrow-right">
    Convert a checklist item into a new card.

    **Description:**
    Converts a checklist item into a new card (useful for promoting a subtask), which inherits some properties from the item; this is irreversible via the API and offers no customization during conversion.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `idCheckItem` – The check item ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Cards Actions Comments By Id Card By Id Action" icon="trash">
    Delete a specific comment from a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Deletes a specific comment action (identified by `idAction`) from a Trello card (identified by `idCard`); this operation is irreversible and only affects comments.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idAction` – The action/comment ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Cards Checklists By Id Card By Id Checklist" icon="trash">
    Permanently delete a checklist from a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Permanently deletes a specific checklist from a Trello card.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Cards Id Labels By Id Card By Id Label" icon="trash">
    Remove a specific label from a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Removes a specific label from a Trello card; the label itself is not deleted from the board, only its association with the card.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idLabel` – The label ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Cards Id Members By Id Card By Id Member" icon="user-minus">
    Remove a member from a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Removes a currently assigned member from a Trello card, affecting only the card's member list and not the member's board membership or overall permissions.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idMember` – The member ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Checklist Item" icon="trash">
    Permanently delete a check item from a checklist.

    **Description:**
    Permanently deletes a specific check item from a checklist on a Trello card; this operation is irreversible and only affects the specified item, not the entire checklist.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `idCheckItem` – The check item ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Checklists By Id Checklist" icon="trash">
    Permanently delete a Trello checklist.

    **Description:**
    Permanently and irreversibly deletes a Trello checklist and all its items using the `idChecklist`.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Boards By Id Board" icon="file-lines">
    Fetch comprehensive details for a specific Trello board.

    **Description:**
    Fetches comprehensive details for a specific Trello board by its ID; this is a read-only action.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idBoard` – The board ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Boards Cards By Id Board" icon="list">
    Retrieve cards from an existing Trello board.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves cards from an existing Trello board, allowing filtering and customization of fields for cards, attachments, and members.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idBoard` – The board ID *(required)*
    - `filter` – Filter cards *(optional)*
    - `fields` – Fields to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Boards Cards By Id Board By Filter" icon="list">
    Retrieve cards from a board filtered by status.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves cards from a specified Trello board, filtered by 'all', 'closed', 'none', 'open', or 'visible'.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idBoard` – The board ID *(required)*
    - `filter` – Filter type (all, closed, none, open, visible) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Boards Cards By Id Board By Id Card" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve details for a specific Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves details for a specific Trello card by its ID and its parent board's ID, with options to customize returned fields for the card and associated data like attachments, actions, members, and checklists.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idBoard` – The board ID *(required)*
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `fields` – Fields to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Boards Labels By Id Board" icon="tags">
    Fetch labels for a specified Trello board.

    **Description:**
    Fetches labels for a specified Trello board, aiding in its organization or label management; this action does not detail per-card label usage.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idBoard` – The board ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Boards Lists By Id Board" icon="list">
    Retrieve lists from a specified Trello board.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves lists from a specified Trello board, with options to filter lists and include card details.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idBoard` – The board ID *(required)*
    - `filter` – Filter lists *(optional)*
    - `cards` – Include card details *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Boards Members By Id Board" icon="users">
    Retrieve members of a Trello board.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves members of a Trello board, with options to filter the list and select specific member fields to return.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idBoard` – The board ID *(required)*
    - `filter` – Filter members *(optional)*
    - `fields` – Fields to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Boards Members Cards By Id Board By Id Member" icon="list">
    Retrieve cards for a member on a board.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves cards for a member on a board, with options to customize returned fields and related data; member must have board access.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idBoard` – The board ID *(required)*
    - `idMember` – The member ID *(required)*
    - `filter` – Filter cards *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Cards Actions By Id Card" icon="clock-rotate-left">
    Retrieve the history of actions for a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves the history of actions (e.g., comments, updates, moves) for a Trello card specified by `idCard`; the card must exist and very old actions might not be available.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `filter` – Filter actions *(optional)*
    - `limit` – Number of results to return *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Cards By Id Card" icon="file-lines">
    Retrieve a Trello card by its ID.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves a Trello card by its ID or shortlink, with options to include related data like actions, attachments, members, and checklists.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `fields` – Fields to return *(optional)*
    - `actions` – Include actions *(optional)*
    - `attachments` – Include attachments *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Cards Check Item States By Id Card" icon="list-check">

    - `fields` – Fields to return *(optional)*

  <Accordion title="Get Cards Members By Id Card" icon="users">

    - `fields` – Fields to return *(optional)*

  <Accordion title="Get Search" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Search Trello content within specified organizations.

    **Description:**
    Searches Trello content (e.g., boards, cards, members) within specified organizations using a query and customizable result fields.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**

    - `idOrganizations` – Organization IDs to search *(optional)*
    - `modelTypes` – Model types to search *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Search Members" icon="magnifying-glass">
    Search Trello members by name, username, or email.

    **Description:**

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**

    - `idBoard` – Board ID to scope search *(optional)*
    - `idOrganization` – Organization ID to scope search *(optional)*

  <Accordion title="Remove Checklist Item From Card By Ids" icon="trash">
    Permanently delete a checklist item from a card.

    **Description:**
    Permanently deletes a specific checklist item from a checklist on a Trello card using their respective IDs.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `idCheckItem` – The check item ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Card Checklist Item Position" icon="arrows-up-down">
    Update the position of a check item within a checklist.

    **Description:**
    Updates the position of a check item within a checklist on a Trello card; the new position can be 'top', 'bottom', or a positive integer.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `idCheckItem` – The check item ID *(required)*
    - `value` – New position (top, bottom, or integer) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Card Checklist Item State By Ids" icon="check">
    Update the state of a check item on a card's checklist.

    **Description:**
    Updates the state of a specific check item on a Trello card's checklist, only affecting its completion status and no other properties.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `idCheckItem` – The check item ID *(required)*
    - `state` – New state (complete or incomplete) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Card Comment" icon="pencil">
    Update the text for a comment on a card.

    **Description:**
    Updates the text for a given comment action (`idAction`) on a specified card (`idCard`), affecting only the text content.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idAction` – The action/comment ID *(required)*
    - `text` – Updated comment text *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Cards By Id Card" icon="pencil">
    Update an existing Trello card's attributes.

    **Description:**
    Updates an existing Trello card's attributes like name, description, due date, members, labels, position, or archives/unarchives it, attaches files, or changes its cover.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Updated name *(optional)*
    - `desc` – Updated description *(optional)*
    - `due` – Updated due date *(optional)*
    - `closed` – Archive/unarchive status *(optional)*
    - Additional card fields *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Cards Closed By Id Card" icon="archive">
    Update the 'closed' status of a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Updates the 'closed' status of an existing Trello card.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `value` – Closed status (true or false) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Cards Desc By Id Card" icon="pencil">
    Update or clear the description of a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Updates or clears the entire description of an existing Trello card; use an empty string for `value` to clear.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `value` – Updated description (empty string to clear) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Cards Due By Id Card" icon="calendar">
    Update the due date of a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Updates the due date of a specific Trello card; the card identified by `idCard` must exist.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `value` – Updated due date *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Cards Id Board By Id Card" icon="arrows-up-down">
    Move a Trello card to a different board.

    **Description:**
    Moves a Trello card to a different board and, optionally, to a specific list on that new board, useful for reorganizing across projects or workflows.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `value` – New board ID *(required)*
    - `idList` – Target list ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Cards Id List By Id Card" icon="arrows-up-down">
    Move a Trello card to a different list.

    **Description:**
    Moves a Trello card to a different list on the same Trello board; this operation is idempotent and only updates the card's list ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `value` – New list ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Cards Id Members By Id Card" icon="user-plus">
    Add a member to a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Adds a member to a Trello card, appending their ID to the card's list of member IDs; the card must exist and the member must have board permissions.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `value` – Member ID to add *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Cards Labels By Id Card" icon="tag">
    Update labels on an existing Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Updates labels on an existing Trello card; use `value` with a color list (e.g., 'red,blue') or 'all' to replace all labels, or `color` and `name` to add/update a specific label (created if new on board with given attributes).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `value` – Label colors or 'all' *(optional)*
    - `name` – Label name *(optional)*
    - `color` – Label color *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Cards Name By Id Card" icon="pencil">
    Update the name of an existing Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Updates the name of an existing Trello card, identified by its ID or shortLink; other card properties remain unchanged.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `value` – Updated card name *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Checklist Item By Ids" icon="pencil">
    Update a check item's attributes or move it to a different checklist.

    **Description:**
    Updates a check item's attributes (name, position, state) or moves it to a different checklist on the same card, requiring the card ID, current checklist ID, and check item ID.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `idCheckItem` – The check item ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Updated name *(optional)*
    - `pos` – Updated position *(optional)*
    - `state` – Updated state *(optional)*
    - `idChecklist` – Target checklist ID for move *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Checklist Item Name In Card" icon="pencil">
    Update the name of a check item on a checklist.

    **Description:**
    Updates the name of a specific check item on a checklist within a Trello card, provided the card, checklist, and check item all exist.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idCard` – The card ID *(required)*
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `idCheckItem` – The check item ID *(required)*
    - `value` – Updated item name *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Checklists By Id Checklist" icon="pencil">
    Update an existing Trello checklist.

    **Description:**
    Updates an existing Trello checklist, allowing modification of its name, position, associated card/board, or copying items from a source checklist.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `name` – Updated name *(optional)*
    - `pos` – Updated position *(optional)*
    - `idCard` – Updated card ID *(optional)*
    - `idBoard` – Updated board ID *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Checklists Name By Id Checklist" icon="pencil">
    Update the name of an existing Trello checklist.

    **Description:**
    Updates the name of an existing Trello checklist.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `value` – Updated checklist name *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Checklists Pos By Id Checklist" icon="arrows-up-down">
    Update the position of a checklist on a Trello card.

    **Description:**
    Updates the position of an existing checklist on a Trello card.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `idChecklist` – The checklist ID *(required)*
    - `value` – New position (top, bottom, or integer) *(required)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Zoho</h2>
</div>

Zoho is a suite of cloud applications including CRM, email marketing, and collaboration tools, enabling businesses to automate and scale operations.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Convert Zoho Lead" icon="arrow-right">
    Convert a lead into a contact, account, and optionally a deal.

    **Description:**
    Converts a lead into a contact, account, and optionally a deal in Zoho CRM.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `lead_id` – The lead ID *(required)*
    - `create_deal` – Create deal flag *(optional)*
    - `deal_fields` – Deal field values *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Create Zoho Record" icon="plus">
    Create new records in a specified module.

    **Description:**
    Creates new records in a specified module in Zoho CRM.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `module` – Module name (e.g., Leads, Contacts, Accounts) *(required)*
    - `data` – Record data fields *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Zoho Records" icon="list">
    Retrieve records from a specified module.

    **Description:**
    Retrieves records from a specified module in Zoho CRM. Notes: - Discrete (page/per_page) pagination is limited to the first 2,000 records. To retrieve records beyond this, use token-based pagination via page_token from the previous response's info.next_page_token. - Do not use page together with page_token. - You cannot use cvid together with sort_by.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `module` – Module name (e.g., Leads, Contacts, Accounts) *(required)*
    - `page` – Page number *(optional)*
    - `per_page` – Records per page *(optional)*
    - `page_token` – Pagination token *(optional)*
    - `sort_by` – Sort field *(optional)*
    - `sort_order` – Sort order *(optional)*
    - `fields` – Fields to retrieve *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Related Records" icon="link">
    Associate or update relationships between records.

    **Description:**
    Associates or updates relationships between records across different modules in Zoho CRM.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `module` – Source module name *(required)*
    - `record_id` – Source record ID *(required)*
    - `related_module` – Related module name *(required)*
    - `related_record_id` – Related record ID *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Zoho Record" icon="pencil">
    Update existing records in a specified module.

    **Description:**
    Updates existing records in a specified module in Zoho CRM.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `module` – Module name (e.g., Leads, Contacts, Accounts) *(required)*
    - `record_id` – The record ID *(required)*
    - `data` – Updated record data fields *(required)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

  style={{

    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
  }}
>
  <img
    src="https://django-outbox-public.s3.amazonaws.com/app_icons/zoho.webp"
    alt="Zoho Bigin"
    style={{ width: "32px", height: "32px", borderRadius: "6px" }}
  />
  <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Zoho Bigin</h2>
</div>

Zoho Bigin is a simplified CRM solution from Zoho tailored for small businesses, focusing on pipeline tracking and relationship management.

**Available Tools:**

<AccordionGroup>
  <Accordion title="Add Records" icon="plus">
    Add new records to a module.

    **Description:**
    Tool to add new records to a module. Use when you need to programmatically insert one or more records into Bigin after confirming module name and field API names. Provide required fields per module (e.g., Contacts requires Last_Name).

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `module` – Module name *(required)*
    - `data` – Record data fields *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Add Tags To Records" icon="tag">
    Add tags to a specific record in a module.

    **Description:**
    Tool to add tags to a specific record in a module. Use when you need to categorize or label a record after creation or update.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `module` – Module name *(required)*
    - `record_id` – The record ID *(required)*
    - `tags` – Tags to add *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Delete Records" icon="trash">
    Delete records from a module.

    **Description:**
    Tool to delete records from a module. Use when removing one or multiple records after confirming their IDs.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `module` – Module name *(required)*
    - `record_ids` – Record IDs to delete *(required)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Get Records" icon="list">
    Retrieve records from a Bigin module.

    **Description:**
    Tool to retrieve records from a Bigin module. Use when listing or querying module data with specific fields, sorting, filtering, and pagination.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `module` – Module name *(required)*
    - `fields` – Fields to retrieve *(optional)*
    - `sort_by` – Sort field *(optional)*
    - `sort_order` – Sort order *(optional)*
    - `page` – Page number *(optional)*
    - `per_page` – Records per page *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

  <Accordion title="Update Records" icon="pencil">
    Update existing records in a module.

    **Description:**
    Tool to update existing records in a module. Use when you need to modify one or multiple records after confirming their IDs and field API names. Supports up to 100 records per call; specify an optional trigger to control workflow execution.

    **Variables (Agent fills during call):**
    - `module` – Module name *(required)*
    - `record_ids` – Record IDs to update *(required)*
    - `data` – Updated record data fields *(required)*
    - `trigger` – Workflow trigger flag *(optional)*

  </Accordion>

</AccordionGroup>

---

<div
  style={{
    display: "flex",
    alignItems: "center",
    gap: "10px",
    marginBottom: "-40px",
